九一八以後的何夫人家庭 262

— 天然

誰不知道何夫人是嶄新人物，誰不知道何夫人是交際之花，（九一八）這一天，恰爲何夫人與何先生結婚滿月之期，賢杭儷剛從西湖度蜜月歸來，纔抵家門，陡聞惡耗，何先生滿腔熱憤，何夫人香涙盈腮。何夫人道：抗敵不如制敵，經濟絶交，制敵的不二法門，我一向是愛好摩登，買東西是很隨便的，所以很多人說我没有愛國心，可是這回的奇恥大辱，使我没齒不忘，我們組織新家庭，今後的服用器物，一槪非買國貨不行，萬一没有國貨，我倆寗使不用。我們定好了一個家約，以後有了小孩子，個個要絶對的服從。目下我一有空間，吾親身便到親戚朋友的家中去勸導他們，一致不用外貨，這一篇大道理，說得何先生點頭稱是，十分敬重這賢明愛國的新夫人。當天何夫人便把家用器具和服裝品等，計畫一下，到了明天，何夫人親正出馬，到國貨商塲中逐一採辦，何夫人家中的面盆和洗滌器具，買的是立鶴牌面盆及一切搪磁器皿。何夫入的化裝品，是三星牌出品，牙膏，香粉，香水，肥皂，色色齊備。新夫婦密月時還是穿的汗衫，轉瞬秋凉，何夫人便置備了五和鵝牌的春秋衫棉毛衫。新房中的帳帘，用的是鴻新布。夫人的服裝，綢布各做一套，綢的是美亞虬縵縐，布的是鴻新的蝴蝶呢。夫人的襪子，是中華第一的墨菊牌出品。夫人纔出商塲，又想起家用的杯子，便採用了亞光的電木杯盆。何先生和她自己用的牙刷，便採用了一心的新出品。忽而又想到天氣冷了，何先生還是帶的一項草帽，便替何先生買了一項華福呢帽。回到家裏，何先生己有公事房出來，起立慰勞，看見夫人買了很多的物品，仔細一看，没有一件不是國貨，没有一件不是精美價廉。何先生笑着對夫人說，你眞能幹，眞有决心，說得到做得到，不要說其他女子都不易做到，老實講，我也不能做到你的本領。何夫人說這有什麽難事，我們只要人人有信心，有毅力，有恒久的精神，一致的做下去，不出十年十五年，敵人的崩潰，一定是可以看到的。言下夫人拿出一袋萊陽梨來孝敬何先生，何先生也拿了中國國貨公司的糖果，來孝敬何夫人，且喫且談，玩賞這可愛的一輪秋月。正是

多情伉儷心腸熱，不雪奇羞恨不休。欲知後二如何，且聽下回分解。

Page 23

1934.09.18

A Painful Discourse on the Third Anniversary of the "September 18th" Incident 1

Shenyang fell, and only three years have passed, yet the painful impression of the September 18th Incident in the minds of most Chinese people within the borders seems to have faded like a historical relic! If today were not September 18th, how many of the four hundred million descendants of the Yellow Emperor would still remember the great shame and humiliation of three years ago? If the majority of Chinese people usually view the September 18th Incident as nothing more than a historical relic, then even participating in the annual commemorative ceremony is just a way to comfort themselves and an embellishment. If sticking a few posters and shouting a few slogans in a memorial hall could accomplish the great task of washing away the shame and avenging the hatred, then sticking posters and shouting slogans would have been something we were good at in the past, and the great Northeast would not have suffered the lament of being submerged. Why would we need this commemorative gesture?

At today's memorial services held in various places, I know there will be those who speak passionately and those who weep bitterly. At that moment, everyone's true feelings are revealed, wishing they could fight the enemy to the death. Even the timid become brave, and the cowardly become resolute! However, as time passes, pleasure-seekers remain the same, revelers remain the same, and those who are indifferent remain the same. Fortunately, it has not been long since the tragedy of the lost provinces, and the wounds inflicted by the enemy are still fresh, so there is still the so-called commemorative ceremony to vent temporary grief and indignation and express a slight sense of animosity towards the enemy. If, over time, the wounds gradually fade, the grief and indignation gradually subside, and the animosity towards the enemy gradually diminishes, it will be difficult to even seek a formal commemoration. Observing the past and examining the future, this situation and this circumstance will inevitably occur. How can we not be saddened!

Today, I dare to suggest to the Chinese people: If we can truly understand the real meaning of commemorating the September 18th Incident, we will surely pay attention to the continuity of the September 18th Incident, viewing every moment from now on as a concrete and microcosmic September 18th Incident and think about how to first avenge the shame. Only then can we firmly recognize the goal we should pursue, ponder deeply, exhaust our wisdom and energy, and prepare for a life-and-death battle with our common enemy, Japan! Once this determination is made, we can temporarily ignore how much our strength can ultimately defeat the enemy. Let us first examine ourselves: How much of our preparatory work has been completed? How much remains unfinished?

My patriotic compatriots should know that military strategy says: "Place yourselves in a position of desperation, and you will survive." If you truly want to accomplish an extraordinary task in an extraordinary time, then the most difficult path is the most straightforward path. Otherwise, if you only know how to take winding detours and follow the path of least resistance, the temporary obstacles may be small, but the dangers that arise will be great. If we are determined to avoid difficulties and seek ease, leading ourselves to destruction, then so be it. Otherwise, actively resisting the enemy should be the primary principle for establishing the nation from now on! And the way to promote and implement this must rely on the development of the national spirit and the strength of a national organization! Do you not see that our Northeast volunteer armies, who have repeatedly fallen and risen, still know how to fight bloody battles and persevere in their struggle, even under the oppression of a strong enemy? Mr. Guo Taiqi, our country's representative to the League of Nations, recently listed the recent battle achievements of the volunteer armies, announcing them to the world. All who heard it were moved, knowing that the warm blood of our compatriots outside the border still remains and that the hearts of the people are not dead. They all expressed their admiration. How can we bear to ignore those brave men who have placed themselves in the forefront to sacrifice for the country without thinking of lending a helping hand? Do you not also see that our economic boycott movement, which is raging like a fire, has repeatedly inflicted heavy blows on the enemy? Knowledgeable people believe that its effectiveness may even surpass guns and cannons. In this autumn of national crisis, how can we not continue to advocate it to fulfill our national duty? All of these things cannot be accomplished by the efforts of one person or a few people in a short period of time. The true value of the so-called national spirit and national organization is thus revealed!

Alas! The autumn wind is bleak, the fallen leaves are scattered, and the nation is in peril. I want to cry but have no tears! Today, what I can tell the people of the country is only this: "Compromising to seek complete safety will ultimately lead to death; active resistance is the path to survival!" I deeply hope that the people of the country will keep this in mind and not make another mistake!

Alas, the Northeast Today! The World 2

Since the Japanese seized our Northeast, they have immediately started to manufacture the puppet state of "Manchukuo." At the same time, they have implemented a Japan-(Manchukuo) controlled economy, sucking the marrow and blood of our Northeast compatriots, driving our Northeast compatriots like cattle and horses, while they themselves occupy the position of supreme emperor, enjoying themselves and reaping the benefits. Our compatriots in the four provinces are crawling under the harsh rule of Japan-(Manchukuo), unable to survive, unable to find death. They are in deep water and hot fire. Fortunately, their patriotic hearts are accumulating day by day, and the underground resistance movement is continuing its efforts without weakening. However, the Japanese have been wantonly destroying them, sparing no effort. Our volunteer armies, who are struggling in hardship and difficulty, are in danger of running out of food and being cut off from aid. This is truly lamentable! On this third anniversary of the September 18th Incident, as we recall the past, our hearts are filled with grief and indignation. We truly have the feeling of wanting to cry without tears, unable to bear to look back. Therefore, I will summarize and state the current situation in the Northeast to inform the people of the country. The rise and fall of a nation is the responsibility of every individual. We should learn from the past and be self-reliant! Although Chu has only three households, it will surely destroy Qin. I hope that our four hundred million descendants of the Yellow Emperor will share this understanding, deal with the enemy, and dare to believe that our bright and shining flag of the Blue Sky and White Sun will eventually fly again between the Black Mountains and White Waters.

1. Politics: All important positions in the puppet government are occupied by the Japanese. The general traitors are all puppets who eat their salaries. The Japanese hold great power and can ask for anything they want. In the administrative organs of the puppet government, the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Communications are especially densely populated by the Japanese. This is because the two ministries are the central hub for manipulating the economy of the puppet state, and they are not comparable to ordinary departments. From this, we can see the painstaking efforts of the Japanese. In addition, although the provincial governors of each province are traitors, they are actually just holding their positions and doing nothing, only following the lead of the Japanese. In the local county governments and other offices, the so-called counselors and subordinates are also filled by the Japanese, and their power far exceeds that of the county magistrates.

Puyi, who went from being the puppet administrator to shamelessly ascending the throne, should have been complacent. However, since ascending the throne, he does not even have the power to stamp seals. Big or small, all matters are controlled by Hishikari, the commander of the Japanese Kwantung Army. Puyi swallows his tears and regrets it, but it is too late.

2. Economy: The currency system in the Northeast was originally extremely chaotic, but the economic foundation was still relatively stable, and the people were not panicked. After the incident, the Japanese formulated a unified currency system for the puppet state and decided to abolish all kinds of paper money previously used in the Northeast by the end of June this year. However, because the general public does not trust the currency of the puppet state and because the initial issuance of the puppet currency was excessive, coupled with the tendency to stop redemption, many people are unwilling to store it casually for fear of following the same disastrous path as the Russian Kerensky notes. The puppet government, recognizing that the factual obstacles were difficult to overcome, decided to postpone the order to abolish the old currency for one year. Furthermore, in terms of taxes, from the beginning of the puppet organization, it had once proclaimed the abolition of harsh and miscellaneous taxes to reduce the burden on the people, but in reality, it has been wantonly levying and extorting taxes in every possible way. In addition, with the disturbances of bandits and the disasters of floods, the rural economy has been completely bankrupted. Last year's harvest was still abundant, and the farmers thought they could barely make ends meet, but unexpectedly, the Japanese manipulated the economy of the entire region, implemented a blockade, banned the export of grain, and imposed heavy taxes on soybeans shipped to Japan. The calculation is so vicious that nothing can be added! Not only that, but the changes in the countries involved in foreign trade in the Northeast have also undergone significant changes compared to before. According to the statistics released by the puppet government, both exports and imports from mainland China have declined sharply, while the proportion of those from Japan has increased significantly. In other words, Japanese goods have gradually driven the goods produced in our mainland China out of the Northeast market in order to realize its controlled economy plan.

3. Opium Disaster: The people of the Northeast have always regarded land and grain as the foundation of their economic activities. Now, the price of grain has fallen sharply, and there are still many who have goods but cannot sell them. Therefore, in people's transactions, opium is often used as a substitute for currency. The number of opium addicts in the Northeast has increased by 70% compared to before. Moreover, in order to increase revenue, the puppet state has openly designated areas for planting opium as places for collecting opium tax. However, the dense forests and mountains of Jilin, which are considered difficult to maintain security, are prohibited from planting. The puppet law stipulates that those who sell more than one tael of opium will be sentenced to six months or two to three years of imprisonment. Those who sell ten or one hundred taels, on the other hand, may be innocent. In addition, the number of narcotics such as red pills, golden pills, heroin, and white powder that flood the Northeast is even greater! This policy of expanding the application of poison is nothing more than a means of weakening the morale of our Northeast people and destroying the physique of our Northeast people.

What is somewhat gratifying is that the volunteer armies of the Northeast have risen and fallen, fighting tirelessly. In recent months, Deng Tiemei's troops have fought in western Liaoning, repeatedly inflicting heavy damage on the Japanese puppets. Liu Liangshan's troops are active on the border between Liaoning and Rehe, Zhao Yushan and others have attacked Bin County, Huang Xishan (Old North Wind) has risen in Benxi, and Qi Zhanjiu's troops are guarding Changshanyu. All of these actions are well-known and praised by our people. The Northeast is now in the season of green crops, and the volunteer armies are taking advantage of the opportunity to operate, and their momentum is even greater than before. The popular uprisings triggered by the Japanese puppets confiscating civilian guns and seizing civilian land have also provided strong support for the volunteer army movement. The Japanese puppets fear that the situation will become a prairie fire that cannot be stopped, and they have always regarded it as a major problem and have repeatedly tried to eliminate it. The puppet Ministry of Military Affairs has recently delineated the areas for suppressing the (bandits) army in order to completely eliminate them. Although our volunteer armies are not afraid of this, they also feel isolated and weak due to the difficulty of receiving supplies. Therefore, providing substantial assistance is our responsibility. I hope that our compatriots within the borders will quickly take action!

The World Situation and the Far Eastern Question, by Ziheng 3

(I) Introduction

Since the end of the last world war, the nations of the world, fearing the dangers of war, have all made a resolute effort to change their ways and strive for international peace. Therefore, all plans that can contribute to peace are being implemented to the best of their ability. Thus, first there was the organization of the League of Nations, then the establishment of the Washington treaties, followed by the signing of the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and finally the establishment of the London Naval Treaty. For more than a decade, the atmosphere of peace has been fluctuating and lingering. At this point, dawn has reappeared. Such a phenomenon has never been seen before in historical records. If we can follow this path and persevere to the end, then even if we cannot say that international war can be eradicated from now on, the fact that world peace will not be destroyed immediately is within the expectations of the world. Unexpectedly, the destruction of peace occurred the year after the end of the London Naval Conference, and the destroyer was Japan, which had signed these international treaties. Isn't this a strange thing?

However, there is also a reason why Japan dares to disregard everything and occupy our Northeast four provinces with violence. The most obvious reasons are about five: (1) The League of Nations itself lacks strength. The League of Nations originally had the sanctions of Article 16 against countries that violated the Covenant. However, in the Sino-Japanese dispute over the Northeast, the League of Nations only made an empty resolution to deny the puppet organization and never dared to impose the sanctions of Article 16 on Japan. This has been deeply criticized by the world. In fact, even if the League of Nations imposed the sanctions of Article 16 on Japan, its effect would only be equal to zero. This is because the implementation of the League of Nations' sanctions must be carried out by strong member states. Looking at the world today, the only countries capable of implementing this kind of sanctions are the United Kingdom, the United States, and Russia. And the sanctions of these three countries must be carried out simultaneously and in coordination to be effective. However, when Japan invaded our three eastern provinces and occupied our Rehe with airplanes and artillery, both the United States and Russia were not members of the League of Nations. (The Soviet Union's joining the League of Nations is a recent event.) In this regard, the reason why the League of Nations could only deny the puppet organization and did not dare to rashly promise sanctions was precisely because it was acting according to its own strength. It is not too much to criticize. If it were not so, its credibility would be even more tarnished than it is today. (2) After the Washington Conference, neither the United Kingdom nor the United States, relying on the strength of one country, could restrain Japan. Although the United Kingdom and the United States each had a ratio of 5:5:3 in battleships, which was superior to Japan, the United States' suspension of the construction of ports in the Philippines meant that it was no longer enough to threaten Japan. At the same time, the United Kingdom, with its defense area too large and no good naval ports north of Singapore, was also not enough to worry Japan. The U.S. naval base in Hawaii is 4,000 nautical miles away from Japan, and the U.K.'s Singapore is 2,900 nautical miles away from Japan. Both distances are outside the effective range of combat. Unless the United Kingdom and the United States cooperate, Japan can win with ease. (3) The confrontation between Soviet Russia and the capitalist countries had not been eliminated around the time of the September 18th Incident. France, in Europe, was acting as the organizer of the anti-Russian united front. The United Kingdom was also very suspicious of Russia. The United States had not yet recognized Russia. Under these circumstances, Japan's direct occupation of the Northeast, under the pretext of defending against Russia's eastward advance, was enough to make the capitalist countries fall into a state of confusion and helplessness. (4) The disputes in Europe, with France and Germany as the core, became increasingly serious. The United Kingdom was constrained by them, making it even more unable to pay attention to matters in the Far East. (5) The United Kingdom and the United States could not coordinate and could not impose sanctions on Japan. These five reasons allowed Japan to be dismissive of everything and do whatever it wanted. Therefore, looking back on the past, the blame for Japan's daring to tear up international peace treaties and defy the world should not be borne solely by the League of Nations, nor should it be borne by any one country. It should be borne by the entire international situation at that time. However, in the past year, the world situation has shown signs of change. The points that can be mentioned are as follows.

(II) Soviet Russia's Accession to the League of Nations and the Far East

When Japan occupied our Northeast with violence, it claimed that if it promoted itself as defending against Russia and opposing communism, it would be able to gain international sympathy. However, it did not know that the speed of Soviet Russia's improvement in international relations was never as obvious as after Japan occupied our Northeast. For example, the extension of the non-aggression treaties between the Baltic countries and Russia, the recognition of Russia by the Little Entente countries, the beginning of Franco-Russian friendship last year, the U.S. recognition of Russia this spring, the recent cooperation between France and Russia, and even today's accession to the League of Nations all occurred after Japan occupied our Northeast. Although the reason for this, in addition to Japan, also includes Germany, which is capable of starting a European war, the main driving force is actually Japan. If Japan had no enmity with Russia, then Germany would not dare to vow to develop eastward. Therefore, the reason why European and American capitalist countries recognize the status of Soviet Russia and even want to encircle Germany with an East European Pact is obviously to eliminate the crisis of a two-pronged attack on Soviet Russia by Japan and Germany, to prevent the further expansion of Japan's invasion, and at the same time to leave a guarantee force for international peace. It is also to increase the power to sanction Japan in the future. Therefore, although the national systems of Soviet Russia and capitalist countries are different today, their interests are connected. The previous state of confrontation can be said to no longer exist. The production of this steady and strange phenomenon is due to Germany's attitude accounting for a small part, and Japan's actions since the September 18th Incident accounting for the majority. Therefore, the impact of this change in the international situation on the future of the Far East is not small.

(III) The Naval Disarmament Conference and the Far East

The formal Naval Disarmament Conference will be held next year, but the preparatory meeting has recently been held in London. Japan's main demands are: first, not to discuss Far Eastern political issues (i.e., the future of the puppet state, i.e., the issue of China's territorial sovereignty and land integrity); second, the issue of naval equality, or the adoption of the total tonnage method. However, judging from European and American telegrams, none of these demands of Japan have been met. The British Conservative Party even deeply regrets the signing of the Washington Treaty and is particularly dissatisfied with the London Naval Disarmament Treaty created by MacDonald. At the same time, it decided to expand its naval and air force plans. The British government also clearly denied the Japanese's one-sided propaganda that Britain had agreed not to raise political issues. As for the United States, it is focusing on air force equipment in Alaska and the Aleutian Islands. At the same time, its former Admiral Pratt has written an article strongly advocating the necessity of discussing political issues. The general idea is that the establishment of the last Washington Naval Disarmament Treaty was originally conditional on the Nine-Power Treaty and the Four-Power Treaty. If the Nine-Power Treaty and the Four-Power Treaty are torn up, then the Five-Power Naval Disarmament Treaty is meaningless. This is because President Harding convened the Washington Conference in 1922 precisely to clear the clouds of war over the Pacific. Unexpectedly, the situation in the Pacific today is a thousand times more dangerous than before. This is precisely the time for us to find a way to correct our past mistakes. How can we put political issues aside and not discuss them? Judging from these two points, the attitude of Britain and the United States towards the necessity of discussing political issues can be said to be consistent. However, Britain and the United States are still discussing issues such as naval ratios and warship sizes. The United Kingdom's desire to restore its status as the leading naval power seems to be very determined. Therefore, it is still impossible for Britain and the United States to fully coordinate. However, the international situation is constantly changing, and the future cannot be predicted.

(IV) The Question of Franco-Italian Alignment and the Far East

A few days ago, a European telegram came, saying that France and Italy also have the possibility of alignment. This news came from Rome, but Paris did not mention it. Not only did it not mention it, but Agence France-Presse also had a telegram denying it. The truth is still unknown. I think that the French and Italian authorities may have this intention because of their common opposition to Germany. However, they are afraid that the United Kingdom will object, so they deliberately released this news to explore the intentions of the United Kingdom. It is also possible that if the United Kingdom can agree, then Germany will become a turtle in a jar, and there will be no possibility of causing a war. Its indirect impact on the Far East goes without saying. However, the key focus is on the United Kingdom. Today, the French consider it a good strategy to strive to obtain British cooperation. They will not disregard the United Kingdom's intentions. Moreover, for France, gaining one Italy and losing one Britain is also harmful and not beneficial. If it is for the Far East, gaining one Italy and losing one Britain is even more detrimental to the overall international situation. Therefore, if the Franco-Italian alignment is approved by Britain, it will be enough to increase peace in the Far East. If not, it will only increase the disputes in the Far East. France is the center of the League of Nations today and has recently allied with Russia. It must consider the status of Soviet Russia in the Far East. If it is not completely secure, it will not align with Italy. Furthermore, France's arrangements against Germany seem to be more than sufficient. The relationship with Italy is good enough. Beyond this, there is really no need to do more.

(V) Pessimism and Optimism

Judging from the above points, although the future of the Far Eastern question still has its pessimistic points, there are also many points that can be considered optimistic. The most obvious point is that today, the only countries that are trying to expand their territory are Germany in Europe and Japan in the Far East. Apart from this, all countries in the world seem to have stopped their ambitions for territory. For example, today's United Kingdom has territories all over the world. Its territory is so large that it exceeds its defense capabilities. Therefore, its status is no different from that of a wealthy family, valuing its life and property. Unless absolutely necessary, it will not want to use a policy of aggression to seek further territorial expansion. If war breaks out again, the British Empire will inevitably face the danger of collapse. Therefore, its policy is to ensure international peace as the best strategy for self-preservation. As for the United States, it has already made a clear statement that it will abandon the Philippines. It will certainly not have any ambition to expand its overseas territory again. France also has many territories. Its greatest requirement in Europe is to maintain treaty benefits. Therefore, its position is also equivalent to a family that is protecting its inheritance. As for Soviet Russia, it has already abandoned its world revolution policy, signed non-aggression treaties with various countries, and now it has joined the League of Nations. Its desire not to invade the territory of others by illegal means is also roughly visible. Therefore, today, the only countries that cannot guarantee that they will have no ambition to expand their land are Japan in the Far East and Germany in Western Europe. But the countries that oppose this kind of attempt include the United Kingdom, the United States, France, and Russia. Therefore, in terms of quantity, the forces of peace have already surpassed the forces of aggression. This can be considered one point for optimism. Furthermore, from the perspective of whether these countries can cooperate, not only can the United States not compromise with Japan, but there is also the possibility of military conflict in the future. Although the relationship between the United Kingdom and the United States cannot be coordinated now, it is very obvious that they will not have military conflict. Therefore, comparing the relationship between Japan and the United States and the relationship between the United Kingdom and the United States, one knows that the relationship between the United Kingdom and the United States is closer than the relationship between the United States and Japan, and the relationship between the United Kingdom and the United States is deeper than the relationship between the United Kingdom and Japan. The reason why the United Kingdom abolished the Anglo-Japanese alliance at the request of the United States at the Washington Conference is this. Compared with the U.S.-Japan relationship today and the U.S.-Japan relationship in the past, the degree of deterioration is really incomparable. Since the United Kingdom resolutely abolished the Anglo-Japanese alliance in the past when the U.S.-Japan relationship was not extremely tense, it should carry out its original intention today when the U.S.-Japan relationship is already extremely tense. Therefore, the rumor that the Anglo-Japanese alliance will be revived is not worth refuting. Some people believe that if the Anglo-Japanese alliance is not revived, the United Kingdom's position in the Far East will be harmed by Japan. However, it is not known that if Japan takes this action, it will only promote the alliance between the United Kingdom and the United States and form Japan's suicide. With the cleverness of the Japanese, how can they not see this? Therefore, although the coordination between the United Kingdom and the United States is not easy to achieve, it can be concluded that the alliance between the United Kingdom and Japan is absolutely difficult to revive. Moreover, the United Kingdom has more than enough self-preservation, which is caused by the international situation. There is really no need to borrow from the Anglo-Japanese alliance. Therefore, in the future international changes, the possibility of coordination between the United Kingdom and the United States is above the possibility of the Anglo-Japanese alliance. This can be doubted. Some people also believe that the Conservative Party of England fears Russia like scorpions, so it is willing to restore the Anglo-Japanese alliance to oppose Russia. However, what the British fear is Russia's world revolution policy. Today's Russia has already abandoned its world revolution policy. Even the weak countries bordering Russia no longer fear Russia. Why say that the great Britain still fears Russia? Moreover, the Soviet Union has now joined the League of Nations, and the power of the United Kingdom is second only to France. Even the East European Pact, which guarantees the western border of the Soviet Union, has been approved by the United Kingdom. Isn't this what the Conservative Party government has done? In this regard, the theory that the Conservative Party fears Russia like a tiger has already lost its timeliness with the changes in the international situation. Therefore, to reiterate, not only is the revival of the Anglo-Japanese alliance impossible, but the cooperation between Britain and Russia has already revealed its beginnings. This can be considered a second point for optimism. Furthermore, the relationship between Britain and France has gradually returned to the old trend of cooperation before the war. Therefore, on the point that Britain must expand its air force, Baldwin does not speak of France, but of Britain's defense, which should be on the other side of the Rhine. The implication is self-evident. What the British fear today is Germany's rash actions. Once Germany acts, a war in the Far East will inevitably follow. Whether the United Kingdom participates or not, it will be harmful and not beneficial. Therefore, for the sake of the United Kingdom, if peace can be achieved, even if it means compromising Germany, it will not hesitate to do so. This is the reason why the British are directly trying to accommodate France. It is also the reason why it is indirectly beneficial to Soviet Russia. It is also the reason why there is still a possibility of cooperation between Britain and Russia. This can be considered a third point for optimism. Finally, the attitude of the United States towards the League of Nations is also gradually changing. If given time, it may even follow in Russia's footsteps and join the League of Nations. If this is the case, then the power of the League of Nations will be thicker, and the hope for peace will be greater.

However, if we want to solve the Northeast problem, there are only two methods: (1) In the League of Nations, the major powers sincerely cooperate and thus implement effective sanctions against Japan; (2) As advocated by the British Labor Party and the Liberal Party, seek the cooperation of the three powers of the United Kingdom, the United States, and Russia to impose sanctions on Japan. We believe that if one of these two methods can be implemented, it will be enough to subdue Japan. The world war can be avoided from then on, which is not impossible.

The Relationship Between Japan and the Soviet Union After the September 18th Incident 4

1. The Situation of Conflict Between Japan and the Soviet Union

After the September 18th Incident, the opposition between Japan and the Soviet Union intensified day by day. The crises that had been lurking everywhere in the past have gathered together as time goes by. Japanese militarists claim to maintain peace in the Far East, but in reality, they are threatening and even destroying peace. The most telling proof is the increase in Japan's military budget over the years. The army and navy budget for this year is estimated at 936 million Japanese yen. The budget for next year (1935) has not yet been determined. Although the Minister of Finance has strongly advocated for cuts to the estimate proposed by the military, we believe that the army and navy will not compromise on reductions. They also have to deal with the Naval Arms Reduction Conference and stabilize the four northeastern provinces. Therefore, the army and navy will insist on their demands. In any case, the military budget for next year will be larger than this year, probably accounting for more than 50% of the total annual expenditure.

The Soviet Union feels the greatest threat from such military expansion, and the situation is most serious in the northern Manchurian plains and eastern and western Siberia. Before the September 18th Incident, the conflict between Japan and the Soviet Union was not direct, and the disputes over North Sea fisheries did not lead to major consequences. After Japan swept through northern Manchuria, a puppet state nominally took charge, but the actual responsibility lies with the Kwantung Army Commander, a three-in-one entity. Heavy troops are stationed along the Chinese Eastern Railway line, and steel and concrete fortresses are being built in the Greater Khingan Mountains. Can such military preparations be reduced in budget?

Japan's military strategy against the Soviet Union originally aimed for (victory without war). The first was to seize the Chinese Eastern Railway at the opportune moment. The second was to use economic offensives to cut the Chinese Eastern Railway into three sections, depriving it of its economic and political value and forcing the Soviet Union to abandon it. Regarding the first method of seizure, the excellent military strength and special political rights within the Northeast were used to direct the puppet state to come forward, which put all actions in an advantageous position. Regarding the second method, the strategy adopted by Japan was more far-reaching. They knew that the Chinese Eastern Railway was deeply rooted in northern Manchuria. If they did not find a way to occupy it, it would not only be a major military obstacle but also cause many unexpected political difficulties. Economically, it was even detrimental to the Japanese Empire. However, if they wanted to use the first policy, they could only act on the eve of war. Therefore, they decided to use the second method to reduce the economic value of the Chinese Eastern Railway so that the Soviet Union would have to retreat. The method they used was to make the Taonan Railway play a role in the western part of the Chinese Eastern Railway, and cooperate with the Siping-Taonan Railway to absorb agricultural products from Heilongjiang as much as possible. They also planned to complete the Er-zhan to Heihe Railway in the shortest possible time, so that the products of Heilongjiang and the Greater Khingan Mountains would be controlled by these two railways. Furthermore, regarding immigration, the focus was on Jiamusi, but now only automobile and summer and autumn water transportation are available, which is very inconvenient. The Mudanjiang to Jiamusi Railway has already started construction. After this railway is completed, the special products of the Songhua River basin will also be under Japanese control. At the same time, the Jihui Railway will also be completed soon. Qingjin and Rajin ports are not only the transit ports for the Jihui Railway but also important strongholds on the Japanese sea. The railway in the Northeast is almost parallel to the Chinese Eastern Railway and has the deep intention of blockading Vladivostok at sea.

The Soviet Union finds it difficult to resolve such political and military threats by force. Economically, it is also in a passive position. If the Chinese Eastern Railway is cut into three sections, everything will be devalued. If the Soviet Union wants to maintain it by force, it will have to use force. However, the Soviet Union is a staunch advocate of pacifism and is unwilling to provoke external challenges, especially to send troops to fight for the Chinese Eastern Railway. Strategically and in terms of practical benefits, it is not cost-effective and unwise. Therefore, it decided to sell the Chinese Eastern Railway to observe the changes in the world political situation. From this, we can see that both Japan and the Soviet Union are engaging in intrigue and each using their diplomatic skills to win future victories without resorting to force.

2. Future Speculation

In this state of tension and relaxation in the relationship between Japan and the Soviet Union, some people are very skeptical, while others are very fearful. Those who are skeptical believe that the resolution of the relationship between Japan and the Soviet Union is closely related to China, and we cannot sit idly by, nor can we take any active countermeasures. Those who are fearful are concerned that the tension between Japan and the Soviet Union will gradually increase. No matter how long it is delayed, war is only a matter of time. Whether they win or lose, it will not be good for our country and is very dangerous. But these speculations are not their fundamental intentions today. Because if they were to start a war with the Soviet Union today, even if they completely occupied the coastal provinces with military force, they would need to send at least 1.5 million troops. Occupying these places would not bring much economic benefit to Japan in reality. The maximum benefit would only be the monopolization of North Sea fisheries and a portion of the forests in northwest Siberia. As for the oil in the northern part of Sakhalin Island, whether Japan can seize it is still a question.

The current Soviet Union is very different from what it was fifteen years ago. When Japan sent troops to Siberia in 1919, the Far Eastern Republic refused to yield. Now, of course, it will resist. If the war drags on, the Soviet Union's base, west of the Ural Mountains, will not be damaged in the slightest. No matter how brave the Japanese army is, it will never be able to cross Chita westward, and its planes will not be able to fly past the west side of Lake Baikal. Conversely, if Japan cannot quickly occupy Vladivostok, the Red Air Force will inevitably threaten Japan's important cities. How can Japan's buildings withstand the bombing of incendiary bombs? Although the Japanese warlords are eager to advance, they are quite clear about this kind of calculation. The reason why they are still vigorously publicizing the tense situation is to consolidate the military and political foundation for occupying the four northeastern provinces. Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations in anger is not beneficial to itself. Moreover, the Soviet Union has recently formally joined the League of Nations, and there will be a major change in the international situation. Japan, of course, cannot continue to interfere arbitrarily.

Since the policy of attacking Siberia cannot be implemented, will they change direction and move westward to obtain wool-producing areas? Although there are many deserts in Inner Mongolia, the southern part of the desert is rich in water and grass, and it does not require much military force or sophisticated weapons. With a little political maneuvering, they can do whatever they want. If the goal is achieved, there are even more important cotton-producing areas that can be seized. This is the main need of Japan's basic industry. Even if major sacrifices are made, it is worth it. Moreover, they estimate the current situation and believe that they can steadily seize it without using force. At this time of complicated relations between Japan and the Soviet Union, we should pay full attention and beware of Japan's strategy of attacking the east and striking the west.

Page 4

Japan's Situation Three Years After the September 18th Incident 5

Although Japan is a late-developing capitalist country, its domestic market still has room for development, and its foreign market has the potential for expansion in neighboring areas. However, since 1929, it has been greatly affected by the economic panic. The lives of ordinary people are directly threatened, and even ordinary industrial capitalists are groaning in pain under the "recession". Therefore, in the summer of 1931, it decided to launch a major incident that shocked the world and was unprecedented. This incident has three effects on Japan: First, it opened up Japan's economic territory and expanded its monopoly market; second, it used the extraordinary period to unite the whole country to subdue the panic at home, suppress so-called democratic politics, abandon parliamentary struggles, and implement military dictatorship; third, as a result of military expansion, large-scale immigration can be realized, and the overcoming of panic and the revitalization of industry will all emerge together, so that Japanese imperialism can be greatly developed.

However, after the September 18th Incident, what is the actual situation? What has Japan gained? Is it really as it hoped? While we are deeply saddened, let's look at ourselves and see what the enemy is really like. Japan's special economic territory in the Far East has indeed expanded, and the development of monopoly industries has surpassed even Germany before the Great War. And because of the intensification of the extraordinary period, the power of monopoly is becoming more and more developed. Naturally, Mitsui, Mitsubishi, Sumitomo, and other financial groups are allowed to operate in the Northeast. Even its domestic industries, such as shipyards, ironworks, sulfuric acid plants, and chemical factories, are directly or indirectly related to military affairs and have gained great benefits. For example, the production of pig iron, which can be used as raw materials for military industries, increased by 31% (in 1933 compared to 1932), steel increased by 26% in the same period, and sulfur increased by 34%. The chemical industry, such as caustic soda, increased by 49.5%. Soda powder increased by 49.8%. Calcium cyanamide increased by 39.4%. Bleaching powder increased by 38.4%. These situations are all factors that activate the Japanese industrial sector and are the origin of improved market conditions. But in reality, the capitalists who benefited, directly or indirectly related to the military industry, and showing the so-called "boom" numbered only 3,000. These 3,000 people, of course, include those monopoly industrial and financial capitalists. The rest of the working masses want to be warm and full but cannot. Ordinary industrial capitalists are still subject to the pressure of economic panic.

Parliamentary politics has never had much power in Japan, and democratic constitutionalism has never shown any merit in Japanese politics. Its political form, the tendency of dictatorship, remained even during the period when democratic thought was at its peak after the European War. In recent years, economic panic has spread throughout the world. If Japan wants to escape this panic, it must do its best to use economic monopoly and strengthen the power of financial capital. Political actions also take the same path, raising the banner of the extraordinary period and making the general public act together under the call of militarism. In addition to the army's large-scale exercises in spring and autumn, there are also large-scale naval exercises. Recently, there have been large-scale air defense exercises in Osaka and Tokyo, making the entire nation nervous, with a strong sense of war, to shift the people's chewing on the pain in their lives. But the general public, especially the industrial workers in the cities and the small and medium farmers in the countryside, are all dying and lifeless as a result of excessive labor. They seem to have nothing to do with the so-called extraordinary period and the so-called national unity. They only feel that the pressure of life is higher than all spiritual stimulation.

Immigrating to "Manchuria" is one of the main goals of Japan's provocation of the September 18th Incident. They believe that with such a vast fertile field in the three northeastern provinces, coupled with Japan's painstaking management over the past twenty-eight years, there should be no problem with immigrating to the Northeast. Moreover, many facilities, military protection, transportation development, and actual economic assistance have been increased. All Japanese who move to the three eastern provinces are lent 1,000 to 2,000 Japanese yen by their government-designated banks to operate agriculture. Moreover, an immigration area is designated in Jiamusi, Jilin, and armed immigrant groups are organized. The Japanese government not only lends them money but also issues self-defense weapons, such as rifles and light machine guns. The protection can be said to be thorough, and the design cannot be considered unelaborate. But from September 18th to now, the number of armed immigrant groups organized is only 2,000, and more than one-third of them have fled back to Japan. Why did this immigration plan fail? First, the climate in the Northeast is not suitable for the life of Japanese people; second, agricultural operation is the hardest work, especially in the semi-developed area of Jiamusi, Northeast, which is even more difficult for Japanese to endure; third, the area for growing rice in the Northeast is not large, and the cultivation of sorghum and soybeans is not familiar to Japanese farmers. Therefore, he used great effort to immigrate, and as a result, only more than 2,000 intellectuals were moved to the puppet state to serve as officials. Most of these officials were also infected with the toxic substance because of the use of toxic policies and became opium addicts and womanizers.

The result of Japan's invasion is that only 3,000 large capitalists in his country have actually benefited, and only a few thousand down-and-out intellectuals have been placed in the puppet state. However, 120,000 soldiers are needed to protect them, and they are all wartime equipment. This is increasing the burden on the general public. It is indeed sacrificing the interests of the entire nation for the convenience of a very few people. Until now, it not only has to continue, but also has to deepen its extent.

Although Japan is known as a newly emerging industrial country, its number of farming households is 5.63 million, and its population is 28 million. Therefore, the rural economy still occupies a very important position. This year, the price of raw silk has fallen, and there is little hope of future sales. The revenue of the spring silkworm harvest for farmers will be lost by 350 million Japanese yen due to the drop in the price of cocoons alone. As a result, the general rural areas have fallen into the misery of starvation. Especially after the price of rice has risen sharply, on the surface, large farmers seem to have gained some benefits, but more than 2.63 million Japanese farmers are small and medium farmers with less than one cho (14.8 acres) of arable land. Their annual income is only enough to keep them warm and full, and there is little surplus. As a result of the extreme decline in the market prices of agricultural products over the years, tenant farmers are exhausted, and self-cultivating farmers are equally overwhelmed. Now, they have to buy rice at a high price with the money they sold grain at a cheap price last year. In the past, the Japanese rural economy of cocoons and a bag of rice was a legitimate and reasonable economic organization. At that time, the farmers only knew that labor was sacred and did not know about economic panic. Now, as a result of hard work, they are even unable to eat enough!

At the end of June this year, the Japan Imperial Agricultural Association investigated that at least 15% to 30% of farmhouses had insufficient rice; and the actual lack of rice was much greater. In particular, in silkworm-raising areas, the lack of rice was as high as 80%. For example, in Ishikawa County, Ibaraki Prefecture (according to a survey by the county agricultural association), 6,021 of the 14,087 farmhouses lacked rice, accounting for 44% of the farmhouses in the county. For example, in Minamisaku County, Nagano Prefecture, although farmers are working hard on the so-called rural self-reliance, most farmhouses eat barley rice; they reluctantly start cutting wheat before it is fully ripe, and many people sell it as soon as it is harvested. In Shizuka Village, Sarushima County, Ibaraki Prefecture, almost all of the 470 households lack rice. In some places belonging to Nagano Prefecture, some even eat tree roots and grass seeds! It is much more serious than four years ago. It is already very common and unsurprising that elementary school teachers cannot get paid and taxes are paid late. This is just a summary of the outline to see a glimpse of the whole. After the Okada Cabinet was formed, it proposed to sell the government's stored rice to the people. In fact, this cannot alleviate the hunger of the farmers, because she is not giving the rice to the farmers, nor is she lending it, but selling it at a lower price. However, it is well known that it is difficult for the average farmer to raise one yen, and it is naturally even more painful to buy rice to eat. Since the rural economy is so declining, the urban industry is also limited to a small number of capitalists who operate military industries. And the vast majority of the people are all floating in the tide of "recession". Because of the fluctuations in life, the general thoughts are also changing drastically. Whether it is the far-right nationalist party or the far-left communist party, they are all dissatisfied with the status quo and have their own reactionary behaviors, which makes the status quo even more uneasy. After the May 15th Inukai Incident, many people were prosecuted by far-right groups such as the Blood Pledge Corps, and their activity is gradually decreasing. Left-leaning thought is spreading particularly widely, and it naturally spreads quickly among workers and peasants. It is not easy for the Japanese government to crack down on it. What it is cracking down on is only a part of the knowledgeable youth and the restriction on publication. In the upper class, children of nobles are also deeply infected with degenerate thoughts and sympathize with the revolution, and even many people actually participate. This is nothing short of showing Japan's own internal contradictions. From real life to thought, everything is undergoing drastic changes. This is indeed Japan's hidden worry.

Central Government Holds National Disaster Commemoration Ceremony on the Third Anniversary of the Fall of Shenyang, Tianjin Public Security Bureau Strengthens Security 6

(Nanjing) The Central Government has scheduled to hold a commemoration ceremony for the third anniversary of the national disaster at 9:00 a.m. on the 18th. The Secretariat has notified the Central Committee members in Nanjing and invited representatives from various agencies to participate. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 17th)

(Nanjing) Representatives from all sectors of the capital have scheduled to hold a (September 18th) national disaster commemoration meeting at the National Grand Theater at 9:00 a.m. on the 18th. The city party department, the municipal government, and agricultural, industrial, commercial, academic, and women's organizations in Beijing will each nominate one person to serve on the presidium, and a letter to fellow countrymen will be issued, with a length of thousands of words and extremely painful language. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 17th)

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Public Security Bureau has strengthened security for September 18th. Since 6:00 p.m. today, security teams have been dispatched with arms, and armored vehicles and mounted patrol teams have been patrolling the Nanshi, Xiguangkai, and Hebei areas. Double police posts will be set up at night. This security is scheduled to be removed on the 19th. (Special dispatch on the 17th)

The Japanese Ambassadors to the US and France Arrived in Peiping Yesterday 13

(Peiping) The Japanese Ambassador to the US, Saito, and the Ambassador to France, Sato Imamura, arrived in Peiping by the newly opened Peiping-Shenyang railway. Sato will go to Qingdao, Jinan, and Shanghai from Tianjin and return to his country by sea. He said he has no comments on the places he passes through due to the limited time. The diplomatic relationship between China and Japan is a delicate issue, and its future direction cannot be solved like a mathematical problem with a fixed formula. To maintain peace in East Asia, the two countries must coexist and prosper. A long period of reconciliation is needed to harmonize the national sentiments of the two countries before the deadlock can be broken and normalcy can be restored. If the Soviet Union joins the League of Nations, it can only be celebrated as a diplomatic success. As for the future outcome, it depends on the changes in the situation. The return of the US Atlantic Fleet to the Pacific is not to threaten Japan; its main purpose is to practice passing through the Panama Canal, but it also contains the intention of preventing accidents from happening in the Far East. Currently, the United States does not have hostile intentions towards Japan. Recently, the United States proposed amending the Immigration Act of 1924, which restricts people of color, and it is expected that the parliament will pass it. In the future, the treatment of ethnic groups in the Far East can be improved. Japan's countermeasures for the naval disarmament conference will not be disclosed before the meeting. However, its general outline has about two main points: to discuss disarmament in the spirit of genuine disarmament, and to seek fair treatment with a fair attitude. Our military and political authorities will hold a banquet at the Jurentang tonight. (17th Special Telegram)

Sun Ke Reports on the Latest International Situation 25

At the Central Memorial Week

(Nanjing) The Central Government held Premier Sun's Memorial Week at 8:00 am on the 17th. Ye Chucang, Sun Ke, Chen Lifu, Ma Chaojun, Wang Luyi, Gu Zhenggang, Li Zonghuang, Chen Ce, Liang Hancao, Wang Qi, Ji Liang, Kexing'e, Zheng Zhannan, Li Ciwen, and all staff members attended, totaling more than 500 people. Sun Ke chaired the meeting and reported on the latest international situation, briefly stating that the United States is currently working hard on economic recovery to solve the economic downturn. For agriculture, due to overproduction of agricultural products, strict austerity measures are being implemented. For industry, strict control of various industries is still being implemented, tightening production, and reducing working hours. This kind of recovery plan is only a temporary solution, not a fundamental solution, because although production is reduced, purchasing power has not increased at all. The effect is yet to be seen, but its trend will undoubtedly lead to a controlled economy as its national policy. As for the situation in Europe, Germany is actually the center. France is afraid that Germany will overthrow the Treaty of Versailles, and Russia is expanding its strength in the areas of Poland and Ukraine. Italy is afraid that Germany will merge Austria-Hungary and encroach on the Balkans. Therefore, France and Russia are working together, and France and Italy have reached an understanding. The Soviet Union's accession to the League of Nations is all about縱横裨　 for its own interests. If Russia joins the League of Nations and cooperates with France, it will be able to concentrate its attention on the Far East. We must not neglect the international situation in our country. After the speech, the ceremony was completed and the meeting was adjourned. Sun then went to the airport and left Beijing for Jiangxi. (17th Central News Agency Telegram)

The League of Nations General Assembly Re-elects Non-Permanent Council Members 33

Turkey, Spain, and Chile are Elected

Our Failure to be Re-elected is a Loss to the League of Nations

The Issue of Russia's Accession is Referred to a Committee for Review

(Geneva) The League of Nations General Assembly considered the re-election of the non-permanent members of the Executive Council this morning. China only received 21 votes and was therefore defeated, as 34 votes were required for election. Turkey was elected as a representative of Asian countries. The General Assembly reconvened at 3:30 pm. Turkey, Chile, and Spain were formally elected as members of the Executive Council. Most representatives believe that China's defeat is a victory for Japan. Unofficial Japanese representatives have been saying here that Japan considers China's re-election to be unfavorable. On the other hand, because Turkey has close relations with Soviet Russia, its election is also a thorn in Japan's side. Soviet Russia's position is strengthened by Turkey's election, and the Franco-Russian group in the League of Nations is also more powerful. It is now heard that at least one country will vote against Soviet Russia's accession to the League of Nations. The Dutch delegation has received instructions from The Hague to vote against Soviet Russia. The Soviet Russian government had previously stated unofficially that it would only consider joining the League of Nations if it received a unanimous vote. However, since the matter has progressed to its current stage, Soviet Russia will not反汗. (17th Reuters Telegram)

(Geneva) This afternoon, the League of Nations elected three non-permanent members of the Executive Council. Chile was elected with 52 votes, Spain with 51 votes, and Turkey with 48 votes, as expected. (17th Reuters Telegram)

(Geneva) Chile, Spain, and Turkey have all been elected as non-permanent members of the Executive Council of the League of Nations. Chile is replacing Panama of the Americas, Spain is being re-elected, and Turkey is replacing China of Asia. (17th Havas Telegram)

(Geneva) China's request to obtain the right to be re-elected as a non-permanent member of the Executive Council of the League of Nations has been rejected by the League of Nations General Assembly. When the General Assembly opened this morning, out of the 52 countries attending the General Assembly, only 21 countries expressed support for China's request to use a roll-call vote. According to the law, it must obtain a two-thirds majority of the General Assembly, namely 35 votes, to pass. Therefore, China's request for re-election was rejected. At this point, Turkey is the only candidate for the Asian seat on the Executive Council of non-permanent members. The General Assembly then raised the issue of the Soviet Union's accession to the League of Nations, which was submitted to the Sixth Committee (ie, the Political Committee) for review. At the same time, the President of the General Assembly, Swedish Foreign Minister Sandler, reported the resolution of the Executive Council, advocating giving the Soviet Union a permanent seat on the Executive Council and asking the General Assembly to approve it. The General Assembly then agreed to take other measures to ensure that the Executive Council's resolution takes effect. (17th Havas Telegram)

Our Country Fails to be Elected as a Non-Permanent Member 34

The League of Nations Becomes More Europeanized

Representative Guo is Very Disappointed

(Geneva) China failed to regain its seat on the Executive Council. The League of Nations General Assembly rejected its request for re-election. Therefore, Turkey's election has no obstacles. Of the 52 countries that voted, China only received 21 votes, which is less than two-thirds or 35 votes. Chinese representative Guo Taiqi criticized this and said, "This is a loss for the League of Nations, not a loss for China. Judging from the results of the voting at the General Assembly, it can be seen that the League of Nations is becoming more and more Europeanized. Many countries that promised to vote for China did not fulfill their promises, especially the South American countries." Since China's election has failed, Turkey, Chile, and Spain can definitely be elected as members of the Executive Council this afternoon. The General Assembly's decision is, of course, disappointing to the Chinese side. However, the Turkish representatives here have known about this result for the past few days, because the Turkish representatives claimed that Turkey has received sufficient assistance to dispel China's hope of re-election. (17th Reuters Telegram)

(Geneva) Guo Taiqi, the chief representative of China attending the League of Nations General Assembly and the Minister to the United Kingdom, recently issued a statement expressing disappointment over the League of Nations General Assembly's rejection of China's re-election as a non-permanent member of the Executive Council. Guo said that in the current environment, the League of Nations General Assembly should give China the right to be re-elected as a member of the Executive Council. In the future, China's inability to attend the Executive Council is deeply concerned that the situation in the Far East will become more serious as a result. Although some Chinese newspapers have mentioned that if China cannot be re-elected as a member of the council, it may withdraw from the League of Nations, but people here believe that China will not take this action. The procedure of the General Assembly regarding China's re-election as a non-permanent member of the Executive Council is as follows: China must obtain a two-thirds majority of the General Assembly to have the right to be re-elected. If China's right to be re-elected has obtained a two-thirds majority, then it only needs a majority of the votes to be elected when electing non-permanent members. If so, China will definitely be elected, and it is undoubtedly that Turkey will be defeated. Now that China has not obtained a two-thirds majority, then Turkey is the only candidate for the Asian seat of a non-permanent member with a majority of the votes. (17th Havas Telegram)

(Geneva) When the League of Nations General Assembly opened this morning, most of the conversations in the General Assembly rest room were about the competition between China and Turkey for the Asian seat of a non-permanent member of the Executive Council. The representatives of the General Assembly were divided into two factions regarding China's re-election. Some representatives advocated adhering to the policies adopted by the League of Nations due to the Sino-Japanese dispute, and supported China's re-election. However, other representatives considered it solely from the perspective of European politics, so they were more inclined towards Turkey. After China's re-election was rejected, people at the scene were quite shocked. Since some delegations to the General Assembly opposed China's re-election, it was generally believed that the re-election of the quasi-permanent members Spain and Poland would also be opposed. Therefore, China's rejection of re-election may affect Spain's re-election. After Spain's re-election was approved by a two-thirds majority, the doubts were dispelled. At this point, Turkey is the only candidate for the Asian seat of non-permanent members, and its election is naturally not a problem. (17th Havas Telegram)

Soviet Union's Accession Has Important Significance 37

(Moscow) The Soviet government's official newspaper, Izvestia, commented on the Soviet Union's agreement to join the League of Nations, saying: "The invitation from the majority of member states of the League of Nations to the Soviet Union to join, and the Soviet Union's acceptance of this invitation, has immense political significance in itself, without a doubt."

Original Purpose of the League of Nations 38

"At the beginning of the formation of the League of Nations, it was an organization of victorious countries. Its sharp edge was directed not only at defeated countries, but also at the first nation of working masses building socialism that was rising at that time, and it was also the target of its arrows. However, the attempt by the victorious capitalist countries to force the Russian workers and peasants to submit to their will was ultimately defeated by the combined efforts of the masses of people under the rule of the former Tsarist Russia."

Soviet Union Strives to Revitalize Itself 39

"Although the Soviet government was surrounded by a capitalist world full of hostility, it was ultimately able to extract our country from the ruins caused by the imperialist world war and guide it into the path of socialist construction. The proletarian revolution and the seventeen-year history of the Soviet Union have now enabled our country's economic, political, and cultural strength to achieve astonishing growth. The Soviet Union is using this growth as a foundation to build its Red Army, which is sufficient to crush any attack and defend this Soviet Union."

Tireless Efforts for Peace 40

"However, the strength of the Soviet Union has not led it into military adventures or the path of what capitalist rumour-mongers call 'Red Imperialism.' The Soviet Union has become the centre of the struggle for peace. It not only extends its hand to its neighbours, signing non-aggression pacts with them, but also participates in all peace conferences convened by the League of Nations, even though the League of Nations still harboured a hostile attitude towards the Soviet Union at that time. The Soviet Union once proposed the most thorough disarmament plan, but it was not accepted. Although the Soviet Union's activities at the Disarmament Conference also had their limitations, it has proven that only the Soviet Union is the only country that can provide adequate guarantees for peace. The Soviet government's policy of peace has even led most of its enemies to acknowledge the sincerity of its peace initiatives."

Two Opposing Camps 41

"The position gained by the Soviet Union's firm policy has created a situation where the majority of member states of the League of Nations now propose that the Soviet Union join the League. At present, the capitalist world is divided into two camps. Some major powers, at this stage in history, are not striving for war because they fear that if war breaks out, their original spoils of war will be lost. Other major powers are extremely dissatisfied with the status quo and are preparing for adventurous actions, seeking a way out of the current situation through war. The withdrawal of Germany and Japan from the League of Nations is precisely to free themselves from the constraints imposed on them by the League of Nations Covenant."

France Can Be Called Prescient 42

"Those major powers that are willing to maintain peace have already realised that if the Soviet Union does not join the League of Nations, their struggle for peace will be in vain. If the League of Nations does not have the participation of this country that acts as a darling of peace, it will not be able to gain the trust of the masses. France can be called prescient among the major powers. It was the first to understand the importance of the Soviet Union in the struggle for peace and initiated the invitation for the Soviet Union to participate in the activities of the League of Nations in order to strengthen the League's peace policy."

Preventing the Outbreak of War 43

"The Soviet Union is aware of all the shortcomings of the League of Nations. These shortcomings are a reflection of the social nature of the representative governments. The Soviet Union knows that the League of Nations has never been able to take any serious steps to safeguard peace in the past. However, the Soviet Union understands that some countries participating in the League of Nations are indeed willing to defend peace. Therefore, the Soviet government views it as its duty to respond to the invitation of the majority of countries in the League of Nations in order to use this international institution, which, as Stalin put it, may, after the withdrawal of some of the countries most inclined to war, become 'a wavering barrier to delay or prevent the outbreak of war,' or 'an obstacle on the road that can at least hinder the arrival of war and contribute somewhat to peace.' The aforementioned words of Stalin are taken from his conversation with the American journalist Duranty. Stalin further stated in that conversation: 'If historical facts develop in this way, then our assistance to the League of Nations (even with its huge shortcomings) is also not entirely impossible.' The development of history has proceeded as Stalin predicted, so the Soviet Union has accepted the League of Nations' invitation."

"In accepting the invitation, the Soviet government has not forgotten to state the fact that some member states of the League of Nations (not to mention those that have already withdrawn) have even more hostility towards countries building socialism than they have fear of war. Therefore, while sincerely welcoming the Soviet government's preparations to join the League of Nations, Soviet public opinion should never forget one sentence: that peace depends primarily on two factors: one is the desire for peace among the masses of all countries in the world, and the other is the strength of the Soviet Union. The stronger the Soviet Union is, and the stronger the Red Army's ability to defend its borders and independence is, the more the imperialist adventurers will fear the implementation of aggressive policies (the ultimate result of which will be their complete annihilation). At the same time, the Soviet Union's position in the struggle for peace will be even more consolidated. The Soviet Union's preparations to join the League of Nations are intended to continue its struggle for peace." (17th TASS Dispatch)

With the Soviet Union's Membership Issue Resolved, European Politicians' Attention Shifts to the Question of Austrian Independence 47

French Foreign Minister is Conducting Diplomatic Activities

The Key to the Success or Failure of the Convention Lies with Britain

(Geneva) Countries are now drafting a convention to guarantee Austria's independence and territorial integrity. The convention is currently being drafted by Italian representative Aloisi, but it has encountered some difficulties on the British side. According to the draft, the convention will first be signed by Britain, France, Italy, and the Little Entente countries (Romania, Czechoslovakia, and Yugoslavia), and then joined by Germany, Hungary, and other countries. Britain's current decision is not to provide any new promises to the continent. Regarding the issue of Austrian independence, Britain, France, and Italy jointly issued a declaration on June 17 this year, expressing the three countries' desire to respect Austria's independence. The British government is currently unwilling to take any further action beyond the aforementioned declaration. Given this situation, the initiators of this convention should first make efforts in London. As for how to guarantee Austria's independence, it is too early to discuss. (16th Havas Dispatch)

(Geneva) The Times' Geneva correspondent commented on the issue of Austrian independence, stating that Foreign Minister Barthou invited Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg, Austrian Foreign Minister Berger-Waldenegg, Belgian Foreign Minister Hymans, Irish Free State President de Valera, Bulgarian Foreign Minister Batzarov, Greek Foreign Minister Maximos, and Romanian Undersecretary of State for Foreign Affairs Radulescu to lunch today. Now that the Soviet Union's membership issue has been resolved, the only remaining issue is Austrian independence. This can be seen from the qualifications of the people invited by Barthou. The issue of Austrian independence occupies a primary position in Geneva politics. What is now being sought is to enhance the existing guarantees for Austrian independence. Italian representative Aloisi is currently conducting research to find a practical way to express the unanimous opinion of the countries in Geneva on this matter. The plan to conclude a convention among Austria's neighbouring countries to guarantee Austria's independence is still under consideration. However, the Little Entente countries believe that the conclusion of this convention will reduce the expectations of the League of Nations. In short, Austria is the key to European peace, and there is no question that its independence must be guaranteed. However, whether the member states of the League of Nations will still ask the League of Nations to provide special protection for Austria, or whether they will establish new methods, is difficult to say at this time. (16th Havas Dispatch)

(Geneva) Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg departed from here at 11:00 AM to return to Vienna. Negotiations on the draft convention to guarantee Austria's independence will continue this week. However, Britain's attitude remains hesitant due to fears of increasing its obligations to the European continent, and the Little Entente countries also have concerns. Therefore, the convention to guarantee Austria's independence seems to be leaning towards the format of the Locarno Treaties, providing guarantees within the scope of the League of Nations, stipulating that if Austria's independence is violated, the League of Nations Council will intervene. In short, this issue is still in the exploratory stage. (17th Havas Dispatch)
