Boiled Water 218

— TK

Remembering Langzhong (Part 2) 219

— Chuanren

I was puzzled and wanted to ask about what was happening, but no one dared to answer me. I paid the bill at the teahouse, lowered my head, and walked straight towards the Temple of Lord Huan.

Speaking of the Temple of Lord Huan, it is truly famous! Who doesn't know that Langzhong Prefecture was the garrison land of Zhang Fei, a famous general of the Shu Han period during the Three Kingdoms era! Even now, Lord Zhang is still mighty and awe-inspiring. Last year, the Red Bandits attacked the other side of the Jialing River, separated from the government troops by only a river. The wealthy people in the city wanted to flee, but they were hesitant. So they asked Lord Zhang to descend to the altar and perform automatic writing to answer questions and help them decide. Lord Zhang firmly replied: (The Red Bandits will definitely not be able to cross the river and enter the city. You don't need to panic and flee. I, Lord Zhang, will survive or perish with the city. You can rest assured!) Therefore, all the officials, gentry, and wealthy people obeyed his orders and were willing to remain under the protection of Lord Zhang's spirit, and they decided not to leave. Later, the Red Bandits did not cross the river and naturally did not enter the city, but retreated. So, amidst the cheers of the masses, they bathed Lord Zhang and changed his clothes, burned incense, and kowtowed to him in succession. However, due to the poverty of the people and the exhaustion of their wealth, they did not rebuild Lord Zhang's temple. This is something that the people of the district are still concerned about!

The Hall of Lord Huan is said to be a Song dynasty building. His statue is said to closely resemble the man himself.

A short stature, a dark and swarthy face, two round eyes that almost popped out - we, who were not born in the Shu Han era, have no way of judging whether it closely resembles him or not. However, the statue of the deity is sculpted in a simple and approachable manner, not as strange and terrifying as on the stage. Behind the statue is a tombstone, and the tomb is built right behind the hall. The tomb itself is naturally very large. Someone told me that the body of Zhang Fei is inside the tomb, while his head was cut off by Fan Jiang, Zhang Da, and others and taken to Yunyang County, where it was later buried. So, Lord Zhang's body and head were separated after death.

These are all beside the point.

Regarding the local products of Langzhong, there is a Pagoda Formula as proof. The formula says:

(Vinegar, preserved eggs, Pinellia ternata koji, white sugar steamed cake, five-spice dried tofu, Sichuan Army Lieutenant General.) The last item is a bit humorous, but it is true that the Lieutenant General of the Army belongs to Sichuan, and this is actually the case, not intentionally promoting local products.

Before leaving, we originally wanted to see the famous sites that the Tang Dynasty poets praised, such as the palace of Prince Lingkui of Lu and the garden of Prince Yuanying of Teng, but the wounds we suffered in our hearts during those two days were already deep, and we were unwilling to be deceived again. Therefore, the memories that Langzhong gave me are just these!

Mr. Village Head (Part 4) 220

— Wang Renshu

Village policeman Dong Sheng, hobbled around the corner. He had a crippled hand, all five fingers cut to an inch long, like ginger joints. But he used to be a helmsman operating the pestle in an oil mill. He had plenty of strength back then. He could carry a two-hundred-pound tree from the top of the mountain to the bottom without using a (short pole). Now, he seemed a bit old. He couldn't sell his strength, so he had to become this village policeman who always ate soldiers' (canned ham) and (tin-packaged cigarettes)!

(This damn job, it's not fit for a human!) Helplessly, Dong Sheng the cripple sighed. (And yet I became one! Sigh! I'm no longer a human! Dog!)

Dong Sheng the cripple, like a mangy dog that had a bucket of hot water splashed on its back and lost all its fur, paced on the street.

(Dong Sheng the cripple! Dong Sheng the cripple!) Mr. Feng Wen suddenly shouted out. Listening to his own shout, it almost sounded like the village head speaking. So he lowered his face and quietly, awkwardly, but seemingly necessarily solemnly, shouted: (Come here!)

Dong Sheng, with his crippled hand, limped over, as if his foot was also crippled.

(What is it, A-Wen!) In terms of seniority, Dong Sheng was an uncle, and Mr. Wen was a nephew. Calling him A-Wen didn't seem offensive. However, no, Mr. Feng Wen cursed in his heart: (Damn it!) Then:

(Did you put up those notices?)

(Which batch?) Dong Sheng the cripple tilted one shoulder and stopped. (There are so many notices now. Today it's some team, tomorrow it's some army… Which batch are you talking about?)

(It's the one that encourages young men to become reserve soldiers.) Mr. Feng Wen felt that his tone was quite calm and generous, just like the district chief spoke to him.

(Oh! Oh! You mean that conscription notice?) Village policeman Dong Sheng closed his eyes and smiled knowingly. (Doing that is like planting radishes in the spring – nobody will go. Nobody will go to throw their lives away. It'll be torn down in less than a day!)

(Torn down!) The village head jumped up, immediately thinking about his position, which had been formally appointed. (That won't do. That won't do! That won't do! It's a matter between you and me. Can you take responsibility for that? I have another one at home. You put it up again! Put it up again!)

Mr. Feng Wen turned back and headed home. Village policeman Dong Sheng limped behind him.

December New Standard Trading Commences Simultaneously

New Standard Gold Settlement Price Calculation Method 222

The settlement price for December gold futures will be determined based on the London gold bullion price listed by the Central Bank. The exchange has not yet disclosed the calculation method. The simple algorithm for calculating the obtained index is recorded below.

(1) Convert the London spot gold listing price to pence, divide by the Shanghai British exchange listing, then multiply by 1.00472, and then multiply by 978 to obtain the standard gold price.

(2) Multiply 1935 by the London pure gold listing price (converted to pence), divide by the Shanghai British exchange, and multiply by 5078 to obtain the standard gold market price.

(3) Multiply 98261 by the London gold price (converted to pence) and divide by the Shanghai British exchange to obtain the standard gold market price.

However, due to China's gold ban and expenses such as shipping and labor, the method has not yet been explicitly specified. The customs gold price listed by the Central Bank on the day can be multiplied by 5078 to obtain the standard gold settlement price.

New York Stock Market Generally Stable 227

According to a report from Xinfeng Foreign Firm, the New York Stock Exchange was generally stable yesterday, except for US Steel, Allied Chemical and Dye, and Western Union Telegraph. Steel stocks weakened due to unconfirmed rumors that the steel and automobile industries would reduce wages. Silk and Tea: The Autumn Silkworms in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Are Damaged by the Weather 238

Pingyao Early Silkworms Stop Spinning Silk The autumn silkworms in the villages near Pingyao have not been well-fed this year. The amount of late silkworms fed has increased slightly. The silkworm ants are going well, but the autumn rains have caused the fire to be delayed during the prime leaf period of the early silkworms. A part has already made cocoons on the cluster, but the heavy thunderstorms a few days ago caused the silkworms in the cluster to stop spinning silk when they heard the thunder. The late silkworms in the third sleep are also not in good condition.

Liyang Late Silkworms Suddenly Have Abdominal Diarrhea The farmers in the four villages of Liyang have been economically distressed this year due to the drought and famine, and the feeding of autumn silkworms has been greatly reduced. After the guidance of the instructors to supplement the late silkworms, the hatching and development are still good. The early gang has already set fire and is preparing to cluster. The late silkworms are in the third sleep and are opening leaves. However, the silkworms have eaten rainy leaves due to the continuous heavy rain, and they all have abdominal diarrhea. Occasionally, softening and other diseases have been found, and the silkworm farmers are pessimistic.

Shuang Gong Silk Exported to India Still Not Weak The demand for Shuang Gong silk in India is still strong, and the export is not weak. This time, the British company's ship exported 32 packages of Shuang Gong silk, including Fulun, etc., to Mumbai.

No European and American Silk Electricity Transferred to Shanghai The European and American raw silk markets are trending weak and quiet, with thick inventories and slow sales. Foreign banks did not move. Although the domestic silk doors are aware that the autumn cocoon harvest is difficult to hope for, the current silk intake is still light, and the market is depressed. There are no transactions in yellow and white silk. The future is extremely bleak.

Chapter Two: Engaging in Business to Enter Civilian Life, Returning to Yongshou, Bidding Farewell, Heavenly Beings Arrive in Chang'an

This made Zhang Jiefu feel a bit embarrassed. It wasn’t good to continue speaking downwards, nor was it good to stop speaking. So, he simply turned his head to look out the window, acting as if he were appreciating the scenery. The car seemed to have reached the top of the plateau, and as they looked ahead, the plateau turned into a plain, stretching out endlessly. In the distance, a red circle appeared, with two roof ridges. The chauffeur in the front seat exclaimed: “Ah! That is the Zhou Mausoleum.” Everyone looked, and the circular line was indeed the newly built red wall, but there wasn't a single green tree to complement the architecture. To the left of the Zhou Mausoleum, there were seven or eight yellow earth houses, serving as the foreground. To the right of the Zhou Mausoleum, dozens of large yellow earth mounds were piled on the plain, presumably ancient tombs, serving as the background. The scenery of the Zhou Mausoleum that everyone had dreamed of before arriving here was completely absent; the scenery they couldn’t have imagined was completely present. While the car was making everyone search for a riddle in their hearts, it continued to speed forward, arriving at the gate of the Zhou Mausoleum's wall. There was a flat area in front of the gate, where about four to five hundred cypress saplings were planted, as if a reforestation movement had taken place here not long ago. However, what was strange was that these cypress saplings were not verdant green but scorched yellow. In front of the nursery, there was a wooden sign, still white and new. The sign read, "National Tree Planting Day and National Tomb Sweeping Commemoration of the Twenty-third Year of the Republic of China." So and so, Dean, so and so, Minister, erected. It hasn't even been two months since Arbor Day, and the saplings are already like this. However, those who came to admire the tomb of King Wen had no time to first notice the saplings outside the gate. What everyone wanted to know was whether there were ancient buildings here. Unexpectedly, after entering the mausoleum gate, they found themselves within a large enclosure, on top of which were three houses resembling temple halls. Although they weren't particularly grand, they looked freshly painted from the outside. (21)

Whose World Is It After All? 244

— Xie Chongshan

It has been three years in the blink of an eye since the Northeast was lost. Perhaps some have long forgotten the (national crisis), and even if they haven't, perhaps they still don't understand what the Japanese have been doing in the Northeast since September 18th. However, I will now briefly mention some of their construction achievements to provide a comparison for our country. Let's see, whose world is the Northeast today after all?

Before September 18th, the South Manchuria Railway was only 1,129 kilometers long, but now the added railway lines have increased to 3,595 kilometers, more than twice as much as two years ago. At the same time, the capital of the Manchuria Railway Company has also increased from 400 million yuan to 800 million yuan.

In addition to the South Manchuria Railway lines, 695 kilometers of new railways have been built.

As for highway construction, as far as what has been completed is concerned, there are already fifty-five roads, totaling 6,800 miles.

In terms of harbors, ports such as Dalian, Andong, Yingkou, as well as Najin, Chongjin, and Unggi, are currently undergoing large-scale repairs or construction.

Since September 18th, 126 new factories have been established, with a total investment of 188.8 million yuan.

As for arsenals, aviation companies, chemical companies, coal mines, iron mines, wool industry, cotton industry, post offices, telegraph offices, all supplies and transportation related to military affairs are being vigorously expanded, improved, and developed there every day.

Oh, how terrible, how terrible!

The Day the News Came 246

— Yiyi Guan Zhu

On the day the news of the violent Japanese bombing of Shenyang City came, everyone seemed to be running madly in the streets, as if the Japanese soldiers had already attacked from Shenyang City to their front. Everyone's hearts were burning, and everyone's blood was boiling. If at that time, someone who was short was walking on the road, they would surely be suspected of being a "Japanese spy" and would be punched!

At that time, I walked to the Baoshan Road area in Zhabei, and I saw that the billboards there were covered with various slogans, such as "(Resist Japanese Goods;)" such as "(Economic Severance;)" such as "(Irreconcilable with Japan;)" such as "(Return Our Rivers and Mountains)"... It was truly dazzling. There were also many more people coming and going than usual, surging back and forth like a tide. Each one was excited, and their faces revealed an expression of indignation, with a great sense of "(Forgetting to eat)."

Alas! Time flies so fast. In the blink of an eye, today is the third anniversary of "(September 18th)!" I can't help but recall three years ago, when the news came, the people's spirit was so激昂 and generous that it is still vivid in my mind. However, how long has it been? The people's spirit has declined to such an extent! The so-called "(Resist Japanese Goods,)" "(Economic Severance,)" isn't it just deceiving people? The so-called "(Return Our Rivers and Mountains,)" then, please look at the great rivers and mountains of the Northeast today. Whose world is it after all? Alas! What more can be said!

Our Lesson 248

— Ji Ping

I am in this continuous gloomy wind and bitter rain, and also encountered the painful third anniversary of "(September 18th)." Naturally, I feel an extraordinarily intense change in my psychology. Recalling the trauma of losing land on "(September 18th)," who wouldn't be worried and want to regain our great rivers and mountains in one go? But without adequate preparation, how can this arduous burden be accomplished in one fell swoop? The national crisis has been going on for three years, and the cause of national rejuvenation and national defense construction is still minimal. If we want to resist Japan and avenge our shame, it is close to a dream! During this period of national crisis, it is not helpful for the people of the country to be drunk and dreamy, nor is it helpful to talk about saving the country. Only by waking up together and learning from the French nation after the Franco-Prussian War in 1870. In those days, the Treaty of Paris, which was concluded under the city, was more humiliating and humiliating than ours. When the deputies of the two states of (Alsace) and (Lorraine) withdrew from the National Assembly, they shed tears and said: (We are willing to awaken our compatriots and resist the treaty that divides the two states of Alsace and Lorraine. We declare the inviolable rights of the two states of Alsace and Lorraine as our constitution and for our ancestors; we swear to sacrifice everything forever to resist the brutal aggressors)! How passionate and majestic this tragic oath is! After the French were severely stimulated, they worked together to plan the country's rejuvenation. Regardless of any political parties, they abandoned their respective political views and united to hold a national conference in Bordeaux, formulating the Bordeaux Convention to save the current national crisis. The whole country, from top to bottom, worked hard, and finally restored the land, washing away the strange shame and great insult of the treaty under the city.

Countrymen! Can this deep lesson be our example?

A Pinch of Salt 250

— (Jie Juan)

Lemons placed separately on salt can last for a long time without drying out.

Mustard powder mixed with burdock and a pinch of salt can make the color last without fading. Furniture made of willow branches can be wiped with salt and water to make it dry and new, and the willow branches can also be straight and not curved. A porcelain bathtub can be washed with salt to restore its original luster.

If there are stains on other porcelain, just wipe it with salt when washing to remove them.

When drinking coffee, add a pinch of salt first for a fragrant aroma.

Where there are snails and slugs, pour a bucket of agricultural salt water to kill the snails and so on.

Scientific Anecdotes

On the Chinese Typeface (Part 1) 251

— Zhang Zhenlu

A small piece of lead type carries the mission of displaying meaning and disseminating culture, while grasping these major functions and destinies. Originally, it was often trampled under the feet of typesetting workers, but it is also worthy of national attention and should be given good favor!

At least seventy or eighty years ago (?), Westerners of the Jesus Church, in order to print Chinese books and other items that promoted their doctrine, studied and made Chinese lead type for movable type application, replacing the clumsy, inflexible, and long-unchanging movable type wood type used by the old method of water-brush printing workers inherited from our country. Our dignified and culturally advanced ancient country, all the main weapons for promoting culture, actually achieved such achievements today, thanks to the merits of our Jesus Christ, Amen!

The most natural condition for making lead type is to make it easy to recognize. Then, those tadpole scripts, bronze inscriptions, seal scripts, and official scripts are only enough for experts to use for research and research, and are not suitable for the actual use of the general public. In that period, all official documents, public announcements, and other texts, all containing permanent characters, the calligraphy was commonly used in (Hongwu style), often seen in nameplates of officials, lanterns, announcements, private boundary stone inscriptions, spirit tablets on tribute tables, inscriptions on coffins and heads, and so on. Many places still use it. The glyph of the Hongwu style is flat, the organization is generally thick and thin, and the four dimensions are clear and sparse, so that the legal lines are not mixed; therefore, this typeface was selected and cast into lead type, and it was changed into a square shape for the needs of work. Later, the public became accustomed to this printed typeface, and simply called the printed typeface (lead typeface).

With the rough and simple, it is necessary to advance to the fine and complex position, which is the inevitable course of human evolution. You see, the characters of their own country printed with lead type in various countries in the East and West have many different typefaces, and there are also very pleasing art typefaces, the so-called fancy typefaces, how lively! And in the decades since our country had lead type, it has always used a kind of Hongwu-style lead type, which seems to hold the general principle of (the sky does not change, the type of lead type does not change). Well, we already have lead type to use, and there is nothing inconvenient about it, so let's just forget it. There are many more important issues that need to be addressed. This kind of industrial competition will never happen; this is also a virtue, called (peace).

However, the line of peace is always inevitable to be broken through. Everyone has been seeing this monotonous Hongwu-style lead type print for decades, how can there not be (tiredness after a long time)? Therefore, twenty years ago, Qu Tangding created the so-called (Ju Zhen Imitation Song Type) of lead type to meet the needs of the times. The Hongwu-style lead type was then distinguished and called (Old Song Type), probably because the Hongwu style originated in the Song Dynasty. The Imitation Song Type has two types: long and square. Its delicate brush strokes and uniform rules make people love its elegance and produce pleasure. It is a pity that the owner who made the lead type in this style entrusted only Zhonghua Book Company to act as the printing agent, which was limited and difficult to popularize. I heard that now his family is also recruiting other agents.

Special Issue of Jiuchang National Goods Department Store

September 18th and Jiuchang National Goods Department Store 252

— Yang An

Today marks the third anniversary of "(September 18th)." Every time we reach this day, we can't help but feel a lot of sadness and bitterness, and we believe that it is the greatest shame in national history. ("If the four provinces are not recovered first, the strange shame will never be washed away.") Some people say angrily: ("One anniversary, the second anniversary, the third anniversary, all are fantasies. We have lived in fantasy for three years, and the lessons we have learned are enough. Our only way out is to repay eye for eye, tooth for tooth, cannon against cannon, and bomber against bomber. We believe that armed self-defense is the only way to maintain national survival.") This statement is not without reason, but we believe that our only way out, from an economic point of view, is to use paper and needle, without foreign goods, one basin and one bowl, without waiting for foreign demand, to eat in our mouths, to wear on our bodies, not to let foreigners and enemies earn our money. We believe that economic self-defense and national goods saving the country can maintain the nation’s eternal survival. We are holding the Jiuchang National Goods Department Store and publishing this special issue of the National Goods Department Store on this painful "(September 18th)" anniversary, so that all citizens and compatriots across the country will never forget this painful "(September 18th)." Never forgetting to promote national goods is the duty of everyone. Only by promoting national goods can we control the enemy's lifeline, and only by using national goods can we maintain the survival of the Chinese nation. Let us think about how much our market has been destroyed by the enemy in the two tragedies from "(September 18th)" to "(January 28th)"? How much has our sales route been hindered by the enemy? How much has our lifeline been trampled on by the enemy? Therefore, people in our national goods industry are all heartbroken and gnashing their teeth at the commemoration of "(September 18th)," which they will never forget once a year.

The Jiuchang National Goods Temporary Department Store was born on the most enthusiastic promotion of the first anniversary of the "(September 18th)" in the twenty-first year. The leaders of the national goods industry were Fang Yixian, Cai Shengbai, Ren Shigang, Fang Jiange, Chen Jixiang, and Xie Bingru. The factories that joined at that time were China Chemical Industry Society, Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, Wuhe Weaving Factory, Zhonghua Enamel Factory, China First Knitting Factory, Huafu Hat Factory, Sanyou Industrial Society, Shengde Weaving Factory, and Yixin Toothbrush Factory. (Now Sanyou Society has withdrawn and changed to Hongxin Dyeing and Weaving Factory, and Shengde Factory has withdrawn and changed to Yaguang Bakelite Factory.) The address of the department store was originally the Qihua Company on Nanjing Road (now Shanghai National Goods Company). After a long preparation, the only national goods department store on Nanjing Road suddenly appeared. In addition to grief and anger, everyone had unspeakable joy and love for this lovely and comforting national goods. Therefore, the record of business was truly beyond expectation. The staff of the department store were so busy that they did not even have time to rest and eat. Sometimes even the manager had to come out in person. This grand occasion was unprecedented in the national goods department store. Some people even thought it was a pity to be temporary. Therefore, it moved the interests of many leaders in the national goods industry and their determination to establish a national goods company. Although the beginning was small, the impact was great. Now, the Chinese National Goods Company and the Shanghai National Goods Company on Nanjing Road shine on each other, and the grand occasion of business can surpass the Three Companies. When drinking water, one must think of the source, and one cannot but give credit to the Jiuchang National Goods Temporary Department Store. The anniversary of September 18th in the twenty-second year happened to be the year of national goods. The Jiuchang leaders continued their previous efforts and opened at the original site of the Saint George Dance Hall in Jing'an Temple, causing a sensation in Huxi, echoing the grand gathering of the Bathing Buddha Festival. Everyone said that the third anniversary should be held in the central area. This year happens to be the year of women's national goods. With the support of Fang Yixian and Li Kangnian from the Chinese National Goods Company, it will be held in the central China National Goods Company on Nanjing Road. It is so unwavering that the industry cooperation will not come to an end, and the beginning of the industry cooperation (referring to the cosmetics industry exhibition) is also like that. The hope for the future of national goods is truly unlimited. It is said that the Jiuchang authorities and employees have made a lot of efforts in one year, and many products have made significant progress in terms of quality and quantity, which can be compared with imported products. And the Chinese National Goods Company can gather the great achievements of various factories and gain the belief of the society. Try to enter it, and the customers you see are all educated ladies and gentlemen, and enthusiastic patriotic people, all of whom are gritting their teeth and vowing not to use enemy goods again. During this "(September 18th)" anniversary, the old place is revisited, and the feeling of enemy hatred and common hatred is deepened. This kind of significance is so profound and so valuable.

Thinking of Gandhi from (September 18th) 253

— Kang Tun

When the cannons of "(September 18th)" shattered a corner of our beautiful rivers and mountains, I, a widow who held the concern of national subjugation, happened to be traveling in India, the equally pitiful (weak and large) India. At that time, I naturally couldn't talk about taking up arms to defend the country. I could only point my hair at the northeast wind.

(What method should be used to save the country?) (What weapons should be used to resist the enemy?) Until now, I, like our mass brothers, have not answered this pressing question that is hung on our lips every day.

At that time, it happened that the Indian saint Gandhi was preparing to go to England to attend the Anglo-Indian Round Table Conference. In the open-air mass meeting in Mumbai, I actually saw the national savior with bare chest and bare feet from among the crowd of thousands. At that time, someone asked Mr. Gandhi what clothes he would wear to represent the Indian people to Great Britain. His answer was:

(I want to be exactly like a representative, not adding or subtracting a point. Of course, I cannot dress up like an Englishman to please people. I am a representative of the Indian National Congress. The National Congress is a representative of the half-dead and shivering Indian people, so I do not want to pretend to be the glamorous costumes of the Indian gentry to cover myself. This piece of cage cloth that can barely cover my body is my most appropriate clothing. If the climate in London allows me to do this, I don’t need to add anything outside this cage cloth.)

Later, he did buy a second-class cabin on a British mail ship, and set off from Mumbai with a few pieces of hand-woven tools and plates used in prison. He also brought homespun wool short shirts, turbans, and homemade leather shoes, local sheep's milk, dried dates, and dried grapes. He arrived in London barefoot, receiving a grand welcome and courtesy.

Whether India's independence is successful or not, and what the effect of Gandhi's revolution is, need not be discussed here. However, his personal example of using national goods and rejecting foreignization should be adopted by nations that are in a similar position of being oppressed and economically backward.

The anniversary of "(September 18th)" has arrived again. (What method should we use to avenge our shame?) (What ceremony should we use to commemorate?) Our cannons are inferior to others; our planes are inferior to others; our machines are inferior to others; our industry and commerce are even more inferior to others. Our infant production is still lagging behind, but our extravagant consumption is rising day by day. The blood of the Northeast volunteer soldiers is still red between the white mountains and black waters!

At least, all our people, the people of all levels, old and young, men and women, should universally use national goods to replace wearing sackcloth and filial piety, as a long-term (mental mourning)!

The 918 Incident and National Products 254

— Ke Ding'an

The three characters "(September 18th)" taken literally, are merely a combination of three different numbers. However, upon closer examination, it is not so simple. It is indeed an ill-omened term. Recalling the events of September 18th, 1931, in Shenyang, fills one with boundless trauma. Only by understanding China can one grasp the meaning of "(September 18th)," and only as Chinese people, are we deserving of bearing this "(September 18th)."

Since the arrival of "(September 18th)" was so swift, effacing it, I know, is exceedingly difficult! If a person gets a new garment and someone stains it, they are bound to feel extremely displeased. Simultaneously, they will harbor animosity towards that person. This is human nature! Now, upon our beautiful Chinese map, someone has arbitrarily placed a large stain. Yet, we, who are most affected, are less concerned than if our own clothes had been stained. We don't even bother to settle the score. What exactly is the reason for this? Know that clothes are merely a personal possession; the nation is the nation of the masses. From this perspective, it can be said that our weakness of "(selfish self-interest)" is completely exposed. Because one person "(pursues selfish self-interest)" it doesn't matter; if ten or a hundred people "(pursue selfish self-interest)" it also doesn't matter. Thus, the public is entirely "(selfishly self-interested)." Although there may be people who deeply understand the situation, there are too many who engage in selfish pursuits, which truly makes one feel pessimistic. At the same time, there are those who raise their arms and shout, charging forward regardless of the tigers and wolves before them. These are the avengers of "(September 18th)."

The cause of "(September 18th)," I believe, should not be blamed on the interests of others. Others delivered their message early, but we, who love to sleep, never wake up. Consider the repeated invasions, what they have added to us. Remember back in 1915, our intelligent gentlemen created "(Promoting National Products)" – I fundamentally oppose adding the words "(Promoting)" to the concept of national products. It should be "(Using)" instead, that would be correct, because "(Promoting)" is too vague – In the long span of twenty years, have national products truly been promoted? If we had resolutely used only what we needed and abstained from imported goods since 1915, and simultaneously had those with assets cooperate to operate factories, specializing in production, then the results after these twenty years, I believe, would not be less than the Five-Year Plan of Soviet Russia! All of this is due to our general congenital deficiencies and forgetful nature. Therefore, the arrival of "(September 18th)" was not without cause! Repeated great disasters and repeated stimuli, although they sacrificed innocent youth, have brought no practical benefit! "(September 18th)" has certainly become a thing of the past. Now, it has already been three full years. However, unfortunate news continues to arrive one after another. Currently, the market is flooded with substandard goods. Petty vendors and businesses are happy to sell them, and buyers, as long as it's cheap, are happy to buy them. It is said that imports have increased significantly compared to the same month last year. This undoubtedly means that our country's money is flowing out.

The creation of "(September 18th)" was originally the laying of our foundation, and others came to celebrate the completion ceremony. The main reason is that we cannot implement "(using national products)," which led to this. Know that those who can impose aggressive measures upon others are very systematic and organized, not acting rashly. Their minds are so meticulous; their plans are so thorough. We commit the great flaw of being blunt and outspoken, thinking that speaking is the same as doing. No wonder we become a laughingstock!

Conversely, if we all practice "(using national products)," and if a particular national product is still lacking, I would rather not use or eat it, showing such determination and perseverance, wouldn't it be a great pleasure if imported goods were shipped back due to lack of demand?

Do we want to erase the shameful three characters of "(September 18th)"? The only method is: (Implement the use of national products).

The Plight of National Products as Territory Falls and Loses its Markets 255

— Shi Ying

The Path to National Salvation 256

— Ba Ling

What day is today? Today is a day of extreme grief and shame for all our compatriots. Alas! Today is actually the third anniversary of the national crisis of "(September 18th)"!

Alas! The national crisis of "(September 18th)," it is so heartbreaking to speak of! For any Chinese person with a shred of conscience, I think probably no one would not be extremely indignant, right? However, what use is mere indignation after all? The lost territories have still not been recovered, and the compatriots of the Northeast Provinces are still living the life of slaves under the iron heel. The puppet organizations have still not been abolished. The thought of this cannot but cause sorrow to arise in the hearts of the concerned!

"(Save the nation)," "(Save the nation)," this is the unanimous cry from top to bottom throughout the country, but how effective is empty shouting and empty calls? The path to national salvation does not lie in high-sounding talk, but in earnest practice! However, which plan is relatively more beneficial to the nation and the people, and more practically effective in the aspect of national salvation, this perhaps still seems to be a question, right?

In my view, the path to national salvation, besides earnestly promoting national products, I'm afraid there is no other good way. Although saving the nation is a multifaceted matter and requires joint efforts in all aspects, comparatively speaking, promoting national products still occupies a very important position.

Therefore, on this third anniversary of the national crisis of "(September 18th)," the author sincerely tells all consumers that from now on, they must have the idea of only buying national products. He advises all merchants that from now on, they must also have the determination to only sell national products. At the same time, he further advises all national product factories that in terms of production, they must strive for the excellence of the goods, the reduction of costs, and the speed of production. If consumers, promoters, and producers can stand on the same battle line and work together and fight together, then the national product movement in China will have a day of success, and at the same time, there will be hope for reducing the degree of national crisis. This is the sincere prayer of the author on the occasion of the third anniversary of the national crisis of "(September 18th)" and the publication of the special issue of the Nine Factories.

Ballad of National Products

Prelude to Using National Products for the Mid-Autumn Festival 257

— Zhang Mengfei

(Ballad of National Products) The moon is especially bright during the Mid-Autumn Festival. A round, bright moon shines on the window frame. Every family offers incense in the courtyard. Snow-white cakes and peaches are neatly arranged. Chang'e in the moon looks down on the world. Seeing the incense smoke swirling, she frowns. This year, the divine land is plagued by chaos and famine. Not knowing the source of the pestilential air and foul smog. Drought demons have arrived in the Jiangzhe region. The crops are withered, with little harvest. Farmers are bankrupt and in extreme distress. The cries of hunger and cold are unbearable to hear. The northeast is about to fall to the enemy. Darkness prevails, with little light. The Yellow River overflows, causing disaster. Houses are swept away, turning the land into a watery realm. Some areas are flooded, while others are arid. Why is Heaven so uneven? Now, in the blink of an eye, the Mid-Autumn Festival arrives. Bills will be sent to every household again. Life is extremely difficult this year. Sadly, all industries are withering. External troubles have not been resolved, and natural disasters arise. How can the people survive? Moreover, the European and American powers are intensifying their armaments. It seems that a major catastrophe is imminent. But the Chinese people should love Chinese goods. Promoting national products is the truth. The Nine Factories Fair is truly lively. The September 18th anniversary is just opening. Everyone comes together to buy. Do not let the rights belong to foreigners. This can also slightly relieve the resentment in your heart.

Wang Zirong (Part 1) 258

— Ding Xing

| Written to commemorate the 918 Incident |

What a vast open space, but the ground is littered with a lot of small stone chips. Originally, this large open space was specially used as an execution ground. I remember that once, thirteen ruthless robbers were beheaded there. Among them, two were truly remarkable fellows. One was beheaded fifteen times, but not only did he not have any marks on his neck, but even the executioner had to be replaced six times, and the executioner's blade was also chipped six times. Another was beheaded eleven times, but they still couldn't behead him. The robber had a smile on his face and was very proud. Later, the executioner greeted him sincerely, and finally managed to tear and chop the two robbers down. This was still a shocking event in the Qing Dynasty. Later, during the Republic, it continued to be used as a place to execute criminals. Generally, people considered that large open space to be an unlucky place, so no one was willing to clean up the remaining bricks and tiles. Unexpectedly, on this day, I don't know why, it was inexplicably crowded with many people, men and women, old and young, I don't know how many. At that time, my watch was exactly three o'clock in the afternoon, not even a minute short. Out of curiosity, I used all my strength to squeeze into the crowd to see what was going on.

Using all the strength of my life, I finally managed to squeeze to the front circle. Who knew that it would have been better not to look. But seeing it aroused my surprise and shock. Actually, the one in the middle was none other than Wang Zirong, the ambitious young man! Only seeing that Wang Zirong, his face flushed, his throat hoarse, was giving a speech there: (To be continued)

A Brief History of the Nine Factories 259

China Chemical Industrial Works

The naming of the Nine Factories Fair is already well known to all circles. Its motive is to commemorate the September 18th Incident, and it was jointly organized by nine major national product manufacturers in 1932. It truly embodies the spirit of enduring hardship and striving for self-improvement, and it serves as a wake-up call for the people of the country to constantly remember the shame that has yet to be washed away, thereby adding stimulation and enlightenment. This year is the third session held, the shame remains the same, and has even become more intensified! What will the people of the country think about this?

China Chemical Industrial Works is also one of the initiating mainstays of the Nine Factories Fair, supporting and urging it, and striving to do its best. Considering that the company has been working hard for 23 years to promote national products and revitalize industry and commerce as its main purpose, its hard work and management to achieve today's status, competing with imported goods, is not something that can be achieved overnight. Its spirit of perseverance is truly worthy of our respect and example.

Furthermore, the company's products can be broadly divided into toothpaste, cosmetics, condiments, mosquito coils, and pharmaceuticals. Each is the first to be researched and manufactured. Therefore, people in the market all praise the "Three Star Brand" products as the "Three Star Old Brand," such as the popularity of Three Star Toothpaste and the excellence of White Jade Cream, which are all praised by people in the community. It is heard that the company has new contributions to cosmetics this year, such as Era Cream, Tianxiang Cream, Soft Fragrant Jade Peony Soap, etc., all of which are cosmetic yarns and products, whose quality is probably not inferior to imported products, and whose prices are far cheaper than imported products. Among the condiments, Guanyin Powder, Wei Sheng, Delicious Monosodium Glutamate, etc., are also sold well in the United States and Southeast Asia. As for Three Star Mosquito Coils, they are sold well both domestically and abroad and are considered unparalleled. Moreover, the company also tries its best to use national products for the raw materials and materials it purchases. Its painstaking efforts are what ordinary national product manufacturers should emulate.

Not forgetting September 18th and only mentioning the Nine Factories Fair, and further linking the Nine Factories Fair to one of its mainstays, the China Chemical Industrial Works, it is not just a matter of praising the company! National salvation and washing away the shame do not originally desire the existence of the shame of September 18th. It is deeply hoped that the Nine Factories Fair will be permanently terminated from the third session onwards. I will offer sincere thanks to each national product factory participating in the Nine Factories Fair.

Meiya Silk Weaving Factory

Chinese silk has always been famous throughout the world, but in recent years, the quality of silkworms has deteriorated day by day, resulting in a gradual decline in production and sales. Since the September 18th Incident, the quantity of raw silk exports has further decreased sharply, and the domestic consumption has also been extremely small. Silk factories and cloth factories have closed down one after another. Farmers have been hoeing mulberry trees and destroying seeds, looking up at the sky and sighing. Everyone knows that this is a major blow to the national economy, and it is a major problem currently facing people's livelihoods. How should it be resolved, then? It cannot be explained in a few words.

Currently, the selling price of domestic silk fabrics has fallen to be similar to that of cloth, and those engaged in the silk industry still cannot achieve the effect of production and sales being equal in proportion. If it is not a loss, it is a closure. There is no day, no time, no place, that is not eagerly hoping for someone to help. The amount of silk produced nationwide is only consumed by one-fifth. The rest is not moved by foreign merchants and is accumulated in the country, resulting in the rural economy becoming increasingly bankrupt, people's purchasing power becoming increasingly weak, and no one paying attention to silk fabrics.

In the past, consumers of silk fabrics in the four northeastern provinces also accounted for a large portion. Since September 18th, this consumption has been taken over by Japanese goods, causing the scope of sales of our silk to shrink day by day. To save the rural villages that have gone bankrupt due to the decline of silk, there is no second way except to try our best to use domestically produced silk. Now that the price of silk is similar to the price of cloth, then using silk cannot be said to be a luxury. So why not use it?

Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, in the autumn of the silk industry's trials and tribulations, with its concentration of talent and capital, therefore upholds its perseverance, is able to support itself alone, and strives to advance courageously and tirelessly, and finally becomes the leader of the national silk weaving industry. All of its products are not only of high quality and low price, but also of many varieties. Recently, in order to commemorate September 18th, it has specially added a large number of products to the September 18th Temporary National Products Fair for sale. Its purpose is to seek the universal use of the people of the country to save the rural villages, and to commemorate the relationship between September 18th and domestic silk, and to encourage itself deeply!

Wuhe Weaving Factory

This factory is a giant in the underwear cotton weaving industry, specializing in the production of Goose Brand underwear. All of its products are of sturdy quality, low prices, and conform to the three principles of being economical, beautiful, and durable. People in the community unanimously praise them and have a good reputation. Here is an introduction to various products for men and women who love to use national products.

In addition to weaving undershirts, tank tops, health shirts and pants, Huhe shirts, spring and autumn shirts and pants, and various kinds of flannel, the factory also introduced a new kind of linen gauze undershirt last year, which is clean, cool, wear-resistant, and washable, and the selling price is low, so it is more than a match for imported goods. Therefore, those who know and those who do not know all take pride in purchasing and using Goose Brand products. This year, the factory also first wove a kind of soft flannel cotton shirt. This shirt has a novel style, is soft and comfortable to wear, and the fineness of the stitching and the beauty of the body make it a top-grade product in underwear. Spring and autumn shirts and Huhe shirts are all suitable clothing for the current cool autumn weather. Therefore, since it was launched on the market, it has been quite popular among young men and women, but the factory leaders are still not satisfied with themselves. They carefully select raw materials, yarn and thread, and strive to improve the engineering and manufacturing, so as to make the products more and more refined. For yarn and thread, if domestic yarn factories have products, they will try their best to find ways to meet the actual needs of (complete national products). On the other hand, they will try their best to keep costs below imported goods to resist the economic aggression of the great powers. At the same time, they will also make the products widely sold, so that the people of our country will know that national product manufacturers can also weave exquisite underwear.

China Enamel Factory

Since the Lifuhe brand of various enamel crying utensils became popular on the market, the enamel products of imported goods have been quite sluggish. Therefore, those who followed suit in the same industry have sprung up like mushrooms after rain, but they soon declined because the successors had no fixed purpose and meticulous methods, resulting in products that were inferior in shape and quality. Therefore, the inventory accumulated and could not be sold.

Lifuhe brand is the trademark of the China Enamel Factory, which is taken from the meaning of sincerity and purity to the extreme, because the crane stands out from the chickens, and is indeed an extraordinary product.

Lifuhe brand's most famous products, such as various European-style washing utensils, sanitary ware, etc., are rare masterpieces in the national enamel industry. The most praised one is the iron box kerosene stove, which has advantages that imported goods do not have. The installed iron box is convenient to carry and beneficial for travel, and it can be welcomed by all walks of life, which is reasonable.

China First Knitting Factory

This factory was established in 1917. The original founder was Mr. Xie Zinan. The main factory is located on Longjiang Road in Yangshupu, and the office is located in Taianfang, Sichuan Road. Initially, it was operated with a small capital. The machinery used internally was all the latest American electric machines, but there were only 24 electric machines, weaving 250 dozen socks per day. At that time, silk glazing, dyeing, etc., had to rely on the assistance of branch factories. After years of expansion and efforts, in addition to expanding the sock weaving department, dyeing department, silk glazing department, box making department, and finishing department, all were added successively, and machines were purchased from European and American countries, so it was able to not rely on other factories, so its products became more and more exquisite, and it has the success of today. Currently, the daily output is more than 3,000 dozen, of which 80% is sold domestically and 20% is sold in Southeast Asia and abroad. The most famous products are Tuanlong brand silk stockings, Tuanlong brand real linen socks, Peacock brand rayon socks, and Chrysanthemum brand mercerized cotton socks. In addition, Yanshou brand and Tiepao brand socks were also popular for a while. The turnover was initially no more than 100,000 yuan per year, and then gradually increased to about 2 million yuan. After September 18th, the northeast market was completely lost. In the January 28th Incident, commerce declined, rural villages went bankrupt, and purchasing power in various places was even worse than before, and the turnover also declined accordingly. The factory leaders thought that the livelihoods of hundreds of workers were worrying, so they tried their best to support it and opened up new markets. The upper and lower levels were united and worked hard to fight, so even in the midst of trials and tribulations, they were still able to support it safely. The turnover this year has therefore improved. It is expected that in one or two years, it may be able to restore the situation before September 18th. The price of goods has been reduced again and again to cater to the psychology of buyers, and the products are required to be exquisite to preserve the original reputation. It is heard that the factory plans to gradually develop various knitted products in the possible period to complete the original intention of the knitting factory and achieve the hope of being the first in China. Therefore, the cause of tomorrow, although half is due to the efforts of the managers, is also half due to the support of patriotic compatriots. Will the future of this factory be smooth?

Huafuli Hat Factory

Huafuli Hat Co., Ltd. was founded in 1918 and is located at No. 50 Hejian Road. The total area of the factory is 45,000 square feet. In order to fundamentally solve the problem, the factory purchases pure quality wool, uses the latest electric motors, self-weaves and self-dyes, and manufactures felt hat embryos, without relying on outsiders, in order to be self-reliant. The products are the Eagle Boat Double Ball trademark. The annual output of felt hats and straw hats reaches more than 400,000 items. The styles are exquisite and the prices are low, which can compete with imported goods. Recently, patriotic compatriots have bought and worn them in groups, and foreigners in general have also praised them for their good quality and low price. It is truly a glorious history in the national felt hat industry.

Hongxin Dyeing and Weaving Factory

Hongxin Dyeing and Weaving Factory was established more than ten years ago. In terms of the dyeing and weaving industry, it can also be said to have a long history. The factory's products are all trademarked with a red star. The intention is very good, because the great light of the red star shines all over the country, that is, wherever the great light of the red star goes, Hongxin cloth also follows.

The only characteristic of Hongxin cloth is that it (never fades) and (the patterns are novel), so it has won the trust of people from all walks of life and is uniformly purchased and used. Whether it is old or young, male or female, all are suitable. It is true that the person in charge of the factory is rich in experience. What kind of material is suitable for the elderly; what kind of material is suitable for children; what kind of material is suitable for old women; what kind of material is suitable for young girls. In this way, its products can win the welcome and trust of the public. The factory currently has more than 300 electric looms and more than 500 workers. The daily output is more than 400 pieces. All major commercial ports in the country have traces of Hongxin never-fading cloth.

The factory's largest special distributor is the cloth department of the China National Products Company of the Shanghai Nanjing Road Continental Commercial Court. Every day, there are dozens of letters from outside the country to the company to purchase Hongxin never-fading cloth.

Yaguang Manufacturing Company

Ebonite utensils have always only been available in foreign goods. The Chinese people buy and use them in groups because of their beautiful shape and because they are not easily broken. Those who leak because of curiosity do not know how many there are.

After Yaguang Manufacturing Company was established, it became famous throughout the country for its ebonite products. The Chinese people deeply felt that the price of foreign goods was high, so they replaced them with Yaguang products. In contrast, the materials of foreign ebonite products were actually below the ebonite utensils produced by Yaguang. The users were in an uproar, secretly lamenting that they were wrong to only admire foreign goods in the past.

After Yaguang's ebonite utensils became popular, there were about a dozen or so companies that quickly caught up. However, Yaguang did not feel discouraged by this. It continued to improve and strive for perfection. Recently, there have also been dozens of kinds of electric jade products, which are crystal clear, like a young girl in her prime. No wonder so many people buy them. It is heard that the company is selling ebonite appliances at special prices to commemorate September 18th, in order to encourage itself with (never forgetting September 18th with every meal) and to warn compatriots.

Yixin Toothbrush Factory

Toothbrush is a necessity for daily use and has a close relationship with hygiene and health. However, in the past, the people in the domestic industry and commerce community considered the matter to be trivial, and few paid attention to it, resulting in a large influx of foreign goods and a large leakage. The owner of the Yixin Toothbrush Factory witnessed this and was heartbroken and worried about it. So he joined forces with like-minded people and raised funds to establish a factory on Huining Road in the Nanshi of this port in 1925. He used new-style machines to start manufacturing. It has been ten years since then. At first, the sales only reached the various ports in the country, and then it reached Southeast Asia and various countries. Wherever there are overseas Chinese, Yixin products are sold. Although the manufacturing is not dare to be said to be excellent, it has been able to gain the enthusiastic promotion of various companies and merchants and the sincere use of people from all walks of life, so that Yixin products have a small place in the national product industry. The factory is truly honored. However, the factory has not dared to be complacent, but has continued to research and improve in order to achieve perfection, so that it can slightly make up for the leakage in case of emergency.

Brief News The China National Products Company (Continental Commercial Court, Nanjing Road), in view of the third anniversary of (September 18th) that has suddenly arrived, must commemorate it. It will be offering a big discount for 14 days starting today. More than 40 departments, each with special discount items, such as silk satin cheongsam trouser material scraps, starting at one cent per piece; electric machine crepe men's robe material, 3.8 yuan per piece; never-fading good wool, 2.8 cents per foot; black grain leather men's shoes, 5.95 yuan per pair; Jinhua southern dates, 9.6 cents per catty; Guan Leming real gold fountain pen, 3 yuan per piece. A special moon cake fair is set up in the south, with all kinds available, which is said to be unprecedented in Shanghai.

Rambling Thoughts on September 18th and National Products 260

— Ji Ping

On this unparalleled national day of remembrance for "(September 18th)," I think all 400 million compatriots, except for infants, have a deep impression. But we Chinese have always had a bad habit of letting things fade with time. As time passes, this impression is faintly forgotten. Just pay attention to the situation of the three anniversaries of "(September 18th)," and you will believe that I am not wrong. When the "(September 18th)" Incident occurred, the whole country was in an uproar, and everyone had the courage to fight to the death. By the second anniversary of "(September 18th)," we only saw slogans of long-term resistance in the newspapers. Now, on the third anniversary, the people's spirit has declined, and they are still singing, dancing, and carrying on as usual. If this continues, I don't know what the situation will be like ten years from now? In fact, patriotism does not require empty talk. For example, when it comes to promoting national products, those who are truly patriotic will always use national products without being persuaded by others. Second-class people will only reluctantly choose national products after being stimulated. The most cold-blooded people will always live on foreign goods, no matter how serious the national crisis is. This is truly what is called "people's hearts are different, each as their face."

Dear compatriots! Look at the international situation, which is so dangerous, and the domestic people's livelihood, which is so difficult; the rural villages, which are so declining; unless they are insane, who would be willing to be a salesperson for foreign goods? Handing over the national treasure to foreigners. Especially in the past two years, the anti-goods movement has completely stopped, and the dumping of × goods is even more terrible than before the national crisis. Just check the figures of × goods imports, and you can know the scattered state of mind of our people and the disregard for shame! I now solemnly inform the people of the country that they should always consider the actual situation after the fall of the four northeastern provinces and the suffering of tens of millions of compatriots who have been brutally ravaged. When spending a penny to buy something, they should first identify the place of origin of the item and immediately make up their mind. If they are still obsessed and recognize the enemy as their father, then they are not human!

Short Story

Mrs. He's Family After September 18th 261

— Tian Ran

Who doesn't know Mrs. He is a brand-new person? Who doesn't know Mrs. He is a social butterfly? On (September 18th), it was precisely the month anniversary of Mrs. He and Mr. He's marriage. The loving couple had just returned from their honeymoon at West Lake, and had just arrived home when they suddenly heard the terrible news. Mr. He was filled with righteous indignation, and Mrs. He's cheeks were wet with fragrant tears. Mrs. He said: "Resisting the enemy is not as good as restraining the enemy. Economic severance is the only way to restrain the enemy. I have always loved being fashionable and bought things very casually, so many people say I have no patriotism. But this time's unprecedented humiliation is unforgettable for me. We are organizing a new family, and from now on, all our clothing and utensils must be domestic products. If there are no domestic products available, we would rather not use them. We have made a family rule that after we have children, each one must absolutely obey." At present, whenever I have free time, I personally go to the homes of relatives and friends to persuade them to unanimously boycott foreign goods. This great principle was said so convincingly that Mr. He nodded in agreement, deeply respecting this virtuous and patriotic new wife. That day, Mrs. He made a plan for the household utensils and clothing items. The next day, Mrs. He personally went to the domestic goods market to purchase them one by one. The washbasins and washing utensils in Mrs. He's home were the Crane Brand washbasins and all enamelware. Mrs. He's cosmetics were produced by the Three Stars Brand, including toothpaste, face powder, perfume, soap, everything complete. The newlyweds wore undershirts during their honeymoon, but soon it turned cool in autumn, so Mrs. He prepared Wuhe Goose Brand autumn shirts and cotton undershirts. The curtains in the new room were made of Hongxin cloth. Mrs. He's clothing included a set each of silk and cloth. The silk was Meiya Qiu Man Crepe, and the cloth was Hongxin Butterfly Wool. Mrs. He's socks were produced by the number one brand in China, Mo Ju (Ink Chrysanthemum) Brand. As Mrs. He was leaving the market, she remembered the cups for household use, so she adopted Yaguang Bakelite cups and basins. The toothbrushes for Mr. He and herself were the new products of Yixin. Suddenly, she thought that the weather was getting cold, and Mr. He was still wearing a straw hat, so she bought Mr. He a Hua Fu wool hat. When she returned home, Mr. He had already come out of his office and stood up to greet her. He saw that Mrs. He had bought a lot of items, and upon closer inspection, none of them were not domestic products, and none of them were not exquisite and inexpensive. Mr. He smiled and said to Mrs. He, "You are really capable, you really have determination, you say what you mean and do what you say. Not to mention that other women would not easily be able to do it, honestly speaking, I would not be able to do what you can." Mrs. He said, "What's so difficult about this? As long as we all have confidence, perseverance, and a persistent spirit, and work together, we will surely see the enemy's collapse in ten or fifteen years." As she spoke, Mrs. He took out a bag of Laiyang pears to honor Mr. He, and Mr. He also took out candy from the China National Goods Company to honor Mrs. He. They ate and talked, admiring the lovely round autumn moon. It is precisely:

Passionate couple with warm hearts, will not rest until the national shame is avenged. If you want to know what happens next, listen to the next installment.
